pythonimport os
import logging
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings("ignore")
logging.getLogger("chromadb").setLevel(logging.ERROR)

import streamlit as st
from dotenv import load_dotenv
from utils.geo_filter import (
    load_geo_data,
    get_all_states,
    get_education_levels,
    is_county_applicable,
    get_counties_for_level,
    filter_schools,
    get_filter_summary
)
from utils.embeddings  import load_vector_db
from agents.orchestrator import orchestrator

load_dotenv()

# ── Page Configuration ─────────────────────────────
st.set_page_config(
    page_title="EduNavigator AI",
    page_icon="🎓",
    layout="wide",
    initial_sidebar_state="expanded"
)

# ── Custom CSS ─────────────────────────────────────
st.markdown("""
<style>
    .main-header {
        background: linear-gradient(135deg, #1e3a5f, #2d6a9f);
        padding: 2rem;
        border-radius: 12px;
        color: white;
        text-align: center;
        margin-bottom: 2rem;
    }
    .main-header h1 { font-size: 2.5rem; margin: 0; font-weight: 700; }
    .main-header p  { font-size: 1.1rem; margin: 0.5rem 0 0; opacity: 0.9; }

    .school-card {
        background: white;
        border: 1px solid #e0e0e0;
        border-radius: 12px;
        padding: 1.2rem;
        margin-bottom: 1rem;
        box-shadow: 0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.06);
    }
    .school-name { font-size:1.2rem; font-weight:700; color:#1e3a5f; margin-bottom:0.3rem; }
    .school-meta { font-size:0.85rem; color:#666; margin-bottom:0.5rem; }
    .school-desc { font-size:0.9rem; color:#444; margin-bottom:0.8rem; line-height:1.5; }
    .chip {
        display:inline-block; background:#f0f4ff; color:#3949ab;
        border-radius:20px; padding:2px 10px; font-size:0.78rem;
        margin:2px; font-weight:500;
    }
    .filter-banner {
        background:#e3f2fd; border-left:4px solid #1565c0;
        padding:0.6rem 1rem; border-radius:0 8px 8px 0;
        color:#1565c0; font-size:0.9rem; margin-bottom:1.2rem;
    }
    .agent-badge {
        display:inline-block; border-radius:20px;
        padding:3px 12px; font-size:0.78rem;
        font-weight:600; margin:2px;
    }
    .badge-librarian  { background:#e8f5e9; color:#2e7d32; }
    .badge-researcher { background:#e3f2fd; color:#1565c0; }
    .badge-docspec    { background:#fce4ec; color:#c62828; }
    .source-web   { background:#fff8e1; border-left:4px solid #f57f17;
                    padding:0.5rem 1rem; border-radius:0 8px 8px 0;
                    margin-bottom:0.8rem; }
    .source-local { background:#e8f5e9; border-left:4px solid #2e7d32;
                    padding:0.5rem 1rem; border-radius:0 8px 8px 0;
                    margin-bottom:0.8rem; }
    .no-results { text-align:center; padding:3rem; color:#999; font-size:1rem; }
    .sidebar-title { font-size:1.1rem; font-weight:700;
                     color:#1e3a5f; margin-bottom:1rem; }
</style>
""", unsafe_allow_html=True)


# ── Load Resources Once ────────────────────────────
@st.cache_resource(show_spinner=False)
def get_resources():
    df         = load_geo_data()
    collection = load_vector_db()
    return df, collection


# ── Rating Helper ──────────────────────────────────
def rating_badge(rating):
    r = float(rating)
    if r >= 9.0:
        color, bg, label = "#2e7d32", "#e8f5e9", "Excellent"
    elif r >= 8.0:
        color, bg, label = "#f57f17", "#fff8e1", "Good"
    else:
        color, bg, label = "#c62828", "#fce4ec", "Average"
    return (
        f'<span style="display:inline-block;background:{bg};color:{color};'
        f'border-radius:20px;padding:2px 12px;font-size:0.85rem;'
        f'font-weight:600;">⭐ {label} {r}/10</span>'
    )


# ── School Card ────────────────────────────────────
def render_school_card(row, match_score=None):
    tuition = (
        "Free (Public)"
        if int(row["tuition_min"]) == 0
        else f"${int(row['tuition_min']):,} - ${int(row['tuition_max']):,}/yr"
    )
    ap_chip = (
        f'<span class="chip">📚 {int(row["ap_courses"])} AP</span>'
        if int(row["ap_courses"]) > 0 else ""
    )
    match_html = (
        f'<span class="chip" style="background:#e8f5e9;color:#2e7d32;">'
        f'🎯 Match: {match_score}%</span>'
        if match_score else ""
    )

    card = (
        '<div class="school-card">'
        '<div class="school-name">🏫 ' + str(row["name"]) + '</div>'
        '<div class="school-meta">📍 ' + str(row["city"]) + ', '
            + str(row["county"]) + ' County, ' + str(row["state"])
            + ' &nbsp;|&nbsp; 🏷️ ' + str(row["type"])
            + ' ' + str(row["level"]) + '</div>'
        '<div class="school-desc">' + str(row["description"]) + '</div>'
        + rating_badge(row["rating"]) + '&nbsp;'
        + match_html + '&nbsp;'
        '<span class="chip">💰 ' + tuition + '</span>'
        '<span class="chip">👥 ' + f'{int(row["student_count"]):,}' + ' students</span>'
        '<span class="chip">👩‍🏫 ' + str(row["teacher_student_ratio"]) + '</span>'
        '<span class="chip">🎭 ' + str(int(row["clubs"])) + ' clubs</span>'
        + ap_chip +
        '<div style="margin-top:0.8rem;padding-top:0.8rem;'
            'border-top:1px solid #f0f0f0;font-size:0.8rem;color:#888;">'
            '🗓️ Deadline: ' + str(row["application_deadline"])
            + ' &nbsp;|&nbsp; 🌐 ' + str(row["website"])
        + '</div>'
        '</div>'
    )
    st.markdown(card, unsafe_allow_html=True)


# ── Agent Badge Display ────────────────────────────
def render_agent_badges(agents_called):
    badges = {
        "Librarian":   ("badge-librarian",  "📚 Librarian"),
        "Researcher":  ("badge-researcher", "🔍 Researcher"),
        "DocSpecialist":("badge-docspec",   "📄 Doc Specialist")
    }
    html = '<div style="margin-bottom:0.8rem;">'
    html += '<span style="font-size:0.8rem;color:#888;">Agents used: </span>'
    for agent in agents_called:
        if agent in badges:
            css, label = badges[agent]
            html += f'<span class="agent-badge {css}">{label}</span> '
    html += '</div>'
    st.markdown(html, unsafe_allow_html=True)


# ── Main App ───────────────────────────────────────
def main():
    # Header
    st.markdown("""
    <div class="main-header">
        <h1>🎓 EduNavigator AI</h1>
        <p>Agentic RAG Framework for Hyper-Local Academic Discovery</p>
    </div>
    """, unsafe_allow_html=True)

    # Load resources
    with st.spinner("Initializing EduNavigator AI..."):
        df, collection = get_resources()

    # ── Sidebar ────────────────────────────────────
    with st.sidebar:
        st.markdown(
            '<div class="sidebar-title">🔍 Search Filters</div>',
            unsafe_allow_html=True
        )

        # Step 1: Education Level
        st.markdown("**Step 1 — Education Level**")
        level_options  = ["Select Level"] + get_education_levels()
        selected_level = st.selectbox(
            "Level", options=level_options,
            label_visibility="collapsed"
        )

        # Step 2: State
        st.markdown("**Step 2 — State**")
        state_options  = ["Select State"] + get_all_states()
        selected_state = st.selectbox(
            "State", options=state_options,
            label_visibility="collapsed"
        )

        # Step 3: County (conditional)
        selected_county = None
        county_active   = (
            selected_level != "Select Level" and
            is_county_applicable(selected_level)
        )
        if county_active:
            st.markdown("**Step 3 — County**")
            counties = get_counties_for_level(
                df, selected_state, selected_level
            )
            if counties:
                selected_county = st.selectbox(
                    "County",
                    options=["All Counties"] + counties,
                    label_visibility="collapsed"
                )
            else:
                if selected_state != "Select State":
                    st.info(f"No {selected_level} data in {selected_state} yet.")
        else:
            if selected_level not in ["Select Level"]:
                st.markdown("**Step 3 — County**")
                st.info(f"Not applicable for {selected_level}.")

        st.divider()

        # Search Query
        st.markdown("**💬 What are you looking for?**")
        search_query = st.text_area(
            "Query",
            placeholder=(
                "e.g. best school with STEM programs\n"
                "e.g. UT Austin computer science fees\n"
                "e.g. Montessori with small class sizes"
            ),
            height=100,
            label_visibility="collapsed"
        )

        # Number of results
        st.markdown("**📊 Results to show**")
        n_results = st.slider(
            "Results", min_value=1,
            max_value=10, value=5,
            label_visibility="collapsed"
        )

        st.divider()

        # PDF Checklist toggle
        st.markdown("**📄 Generate PDF Checklist**")
        generate_pdf = st.toggle(
            "Generate application checklist PDF",
            value=False
        )
        pdf_school = None
        if generate_pdf:
            pdf_school = st.text_input(
                "School name for checklist",
                placeholder="e.g. UT Austin"
            )

        st.divider()

        # Search button
        search_clicked = st.button(
            "🚀 Search with AI",
            use_container_width=True,
            type="primary"
        )

    # ── Main Content ───────────────────────────────
    filters_ready = (
        selected_level != "Select Level" and
        selected_state != "Select State"
    )

    if not filters_ready:
        # Welcome screen
        col1, col2, col3 = st.columns(3)
        with col1:
            st.info("**Step 1**\n\nSelect education level to begin.")
        with col2:
            st.info("**Step 2**\n\nChoose your target state.")
        with col3:
            st.info("**Step 3**\n\nFor K-12, pick a county for local results.")

        st.markdown("---")
        st.markdown("### 📊 Platform Overview")
        c1, c2, c3, c4 = st.columns(4)
        c1.metric("Schools in DB",     len(df))
        c2.metric("States Covered",    df["state"].nunique())
        c3.metric("Education Levels",  df["level"].nunique())
        c4.metric("Avg Rating",        f"{df['rating'].mean():.1f}/10")

        st.markdown("---")
        st.markdown("### 🤖 How EduNavigator AI Works")
        a1, a2, a3 = st.columns(3)
        with a1:
            st.markdown("""
            **📚 Librarian Agent**
            Searches local vector database using semantic AI matching.
            Fast and precise for known schools.
            """)
        with a2:
            st.markdown("""
            **🔍 Researcher Agent**
            Searches the live web when local data is insufficient.
            Finds any school anywhere in real time.
            """)
        with a3:
            st.markdown("""
            **📄 Doc Specialist Agent**
            Generates personalized PDF application checklists
            with deadlines, requirements and pro tips.
            """)

    else:
        # Filter summary
        summary = get_filter_summary(
            selected_state, selected_level, selected_county
        )
        st.markdown(
            f'<div class="filter-banner">📍 {summary}</div>',
            unsafe_allow_html=True
        )

        if search_clicked and search_query.strip():
            # ── AI Search Mode ─────────────────────
            st.markdown(
                f"### 🤖 AI Results for: *\"{search_query}\"*"
            )

            with st.spinner("🤖 AI agents working..."):
                result = orchestrator(
                    collection   = collection,
                    query        = search_query,
                    state        = selected_state,
                    level        = selected_level,
                    county       = selected_county,
                    n_results    = n_results,
                    generate_pdf = generate_pdf and bool(pdf_school),
                    school_name  = pdf_school
                )

            # Agent badges
            render_agent_badges(result["agents_called"])

            # ── Local Results ──────────────────────
            if result["schools"] and result["local_summary"]:
                st.markdown(
                    '<div class="source-local">'
                    '📚 <strong>Local Database Results</strong>'
                    '</div>',
                    unsafe_allow_html=True
                )
                with st.expander("📝 AI Analysis", expanded=True):
                    st.markdown(result["local_summary"])

                st.markdown("#### Matching Schools")
                filtered_df = filter_schools(
                    df,
                    state  = selected_state,
                    level  = selected_level,
                    county = selected_county
                )
                for school_meta in result["schools"]:
                    match_row = filtered_df[
                        filtered_df["name"] == school_meta["name"]
                    ]
                    if not match_row.empty:
                        render_school_card(match_row.iloc[0])

            # ── Web Results ────────────────────────
            if result["web_summary"]:
                st.markdown(
                    '<div class="source-web">'
                    '🔍 <strong>Live Web Research Results</strong>'
                    '</div>',
                    unsafe_allow_html=True
                )
                with st.expander("🌐 Web Research Summary", expanded=True):
                    st.markdown(result["web_summary"])

                if result["web_sources"]:
                    st.markdown("#### Sources")
                    for src in result["web_sources"]:
                        st.markdown(
                            f"- [{src['title'][:70]}]({src['url']})"
                        )

            # ── PDF Result ─────────────────────────
            if result["pdf_result"] and result["pdf_result"]["filepath"]:
                st.markdown("---")
                st.markdown("### 📄 Application Checklist")
                pdf_path = result["pdf_result"]["filepath"]

                col_info, col_btn = st.columns([3, 1])
                with col_info:
                    total = sum(
                        len(v) for v in
                        result["pdf_result"]["checklist"].values()
                    )
                    st.success(
                        f"✅ PDF checklist generated for "
                        f"**{result['pdf_result']['school_name']}** "
                        f"with **{total} items**"
                    )
                with col_btn:
                    with open(pdf_path, "rb") as f:
                        st.download_button(
                            label="📥 Download PDF",
                            data=f,
                            file_name=os.path.basename(pdf_path),
                            mime="application/pdf",
                            use_container_width=True
                        )

                # Show checklist preview
                with st.expander("👀 Preview Checklist", expanded=False):
                    for section, items in result["pdf_result"]["checklist"].items():
                        if items:
                            st.markdown(f"**{section}**")
                            for item in items:
                                st.markdown(f"- ☐ {item}")

            # ── No results at all ──────────────────
            if not result["schools"] and not result["web_summary"]:
                st.markdown(
                    '<div class="no-results">'
                    '🔍 No results found. Try different keywords or filters.'
                    '</div>',
                    unsafe_allow_html=True
                )

        else:
            # ── Browse Mode ────────────────────────
            filtered_df = filter_schools(
                df,
                state  = selected_state,
                level  = selected_level,
                county = selected_county
            )
            if len(filtered_df) > 0:
                c1, c2, c3, c4 = st.columns(4)
                c1.metric("Found",        len(filtered_df))
                c2.metric("Avg Rating",   f"{filtered_df['rating'].mean():.1f}/10")
                c3.metric("Top Rated",
                    filtered_df["name"].iloc[filtered_df["rating"].argmax()])
                c4.metric("Public",
                    len(filtered_df[filtered_df["type"] == "Public"]))

                st.markdown("---")
                st.markdown(
                    f"### 🏫 {len(filtered_df)} {selected_level} "
                    f"schools found"
                )
                st.caption(
                    "💡 Tip: Enter a search query in the sidebar "
                    "for AI-powered matching and web research"
                )
                sorted_df = filtered_df.sort_values(
                    "rating", ascending=False
                ).reset_index(drop=True)
                for _, row in sorted_df.iterrows():
                    render_school_card(row)
            else:
                st.markdown(
                    '<div class="no-results">'
                    '🏫 No schools found for these filters.<br>'
                    '<small>Try a different state or county.</small>'
                    '</div>',
                    unsafe_allow_html=True
                )


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

Fix 2 — Update utils/geo_filter.py
The filter logic needs updating so that when a state has no local data, it still works and falls back to the Researcher Agent. Replace the entire file:
pythonimport pandas as pd

ALL_US_STATES = [
    "Alabama", "Alaska", "Arizona", "Arkansas", "California",
    "Colorado", "Connecticut", "Delaware", "Florida", "Georgia",
    "Hawaii", "Idaho", "Illinois", "Indiana", "Iowa",
    "Kansas", "Kentucky", "Louisiana", "Maine", "Maryland",
    "Massachusetts", "Michigan", "Minnesota", "Mississippi", "Missouri",
    "Montana", "Nebraska", "Nevada", "New Hampshire", "New Jersey",
    "New Mexico", "New York", "North Carolina", "North Dakota", "Ohio",
    "Oklahoma", "Oregon", "Pennsylvania", "Rhode Island", "South Carolina",
    "South Dakota", "Tennessee", "Texas", "Utah", "Vermont",
    "Virginia", "Washington", "West Virginia", "Wisconsin", "Wyoming"
]

STATE_LEVEL_EDUCATION  = ["University", "Community College"]
COUNTY_LEVEL_EDUCATION = ["High School", "Elementary", "Preschool", "Middle School"]


def load_geo_data(csv_path="data/schools.csv"):
    return pd.read_csv(csv_path)


def get_all_states():
    return ALL_US_STATES


def get_education_levels():
    return [
        "Preschool",
        "Elementary",
        "Middle School",
        "High School",
        "Community College",
        "University"
    ]


def is_county_applicable(level):
    return level in COUNTY_LEVEL_EDUCATION


def get_counties_for_level(df, state, level):
    """Return counties only if education level supports county filtering."""
    if not is_county_applicable(level):
        return []
    if not state or state == "Select State":
        return []
    filtered = df[
        (df["state"] == state) &
        (df["level"] == level)
    ]
    return sorted(filtered["county"].dropna().unique().tolist())


def has_local_data(df, state, level):
    """
    Check if local database has any data
    for the given state and level combination.
    """
    filtered = df[
        (df["state"] == state) &
        (df["level"] == level)
    ]
    return len(filtered) > 0


def filter_schools(df, state=None, level=None, county=None):
    """
    Apply filters. Returns empty dataframe
    (not None) if no local data exists —
    this signals the Orchestrator to use
    the Researcher Agent instead.
    """
    filtered = df.copy()

    if level and level != "Select Level":
        filtered = filtered[filtered["level"] == level]

    if state and state != "Select State":
        filtered = filtered[filtered["state"] == state]

    if is_county_applicable(level):
        if county and county not in ["Select County", "All Counties"]:
            filtered = filtered[filtered["county"] == county]

    return filtered.reset_index(drop=True)


def get_filter_summary(state, level, county=None):
    if not state or not level:
        return "Please select filters to begin."
    if is_county_applicable(level):
        if county and county not in ["Select County", "All Counties"]:
            return f"Showing {level} schools in {county} County, {state}"
        return f"Showing {level} schools in {state} (all counties)"
    return f"Showing {level} institutions in {state}"
Save (Ctrl + S).

Fix 3 — Update the Orchestrator
The Orchestrator needs to automatically trigger the Researcher Agent when no local data exists for a selected state. Open agents/orchestrator.py and replace the entire file:
pythonimport os
import logging
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings("ignore")
logging.getLogger("chromadb").setLevel(logging.ERROR)

from dotenv import load_dotenv
from agents.librarian_agent      import librarian_agent
from agents.researcher_agent     import researcher_agent
from agents.doc_specialist_agent import doc_specialist_agent
from utils.geo_filter            import has_local_data, filter_schools

load_dotenv()

MIN_LOCAL_RESULTS = 2


def orchestrator(
    collection,
    query,
    state        = None,
    level        = None,
    county       = None,
    n_results    = 5,
    generate_pdf = False,
    school_name  = None,
    df           = None
):
    print("\n" + "=" * 55)
    print("🎯 ORCHESTRATOR ACTIVATED")
    print(f"   Query  : {query}")
    print(f"   State  : {state}  |  Level : {level}")
    print("=" * 55)

    response = {
        "source":        None,
        "schools":       [],
        "local_summary": "",
        "web_summary":   "",
        "web_sources":   [],
        "pdf_result":    None,
        "query":         query,
        "filters_used":  {"state": state, "level": level, "county": county},
        "agents_called": [],
        "has_local_data": False
    }

    # ── Build filters ──────────────────────────────
    filters = {}
    if state:
        filters["state"] = state
    if level:
        filters["level"] = level
    if county and county not in ["All Counties", "Select County"]:
        filters["county"] = county

    # ── Check if local DB has data for this state ──
    local_data_exists = False
    if df is not None and state and level:
        local_data_exists = has_local_data(df, state, level)
    response["has_local_data"] = local_data_exists

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    # STEP 1 — Librarian Agent
    # Only call if local data exists for this state
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    if local_data_exists:
        print("\n📋 Step 1: Calling Librarian Agent...")
        librarian_result = librarian_agent(
            collection = collection,
            query      = query,
            filters    = filters,
            n_results  = n_results
        )
        response["agents_called"].append("Librarian")
        response["schools"]       = librarian_result["schools"]
        response["local_summary"] = librarian_result["summary"]
        local_count               = len(librarian_result["schools"])
        print(f"   📊 Local results: {local_count}")
    else:
        local_count = 0
        print(f"\n   ℹ️ No local data for {level} in {state}.")
        print("      Will use Researcher Agent.")

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    # STEP 2 — Researcher Agent
    # Triggered when:
    #   a) No local data for selected state/level
    #   b) Fewer than MIN_LOCAL_RESULTS found
    #   c) Query contains a specific school name
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    specific_keywords = [
        "ut austin", "university of texas austin",
        "harvard", "stanford", "mit", "yale", "princeton",
        "texas tech", "baylor", "rice university",
        "tcu", "texas christian", "duke", "vanderbilt",
        "georgetown", "notre dame", "emory", "tulane"
    ]
    query_lower        = query.lower()
    is_specific_school = any(kw in query_lower for kw in specific_keywords)

    needs_web = (
        not local_data_exists or
        local_count < MIN_LOCAL_RESULTS or
        is_specific_school
    )

    if needs_web:
        if not local_data_exists:
            reason = f"no local data for {level} in {state}"
        elif is_specific_school:
            reason = "specific school detected"
        else:
            reason = f"only {local_count} local results"

        print(f"\n📋 Step 2: Calling Researcher Agent ({reason})...")
        researcher_result = researcher_agent(
            query     = query,
            state     = state,
            level     = level,
            n_results = n_results
        )
        response["agents_called"].append("Researcher")
        response["web_summary"] = researcher_result["summary"]
        response["web_sources"] = researcher_result["sources"]
        response["source"]      = "both" if local_count > 0 else "web"
    else:
        print(f"\n   ✅ Sufficient local data. Skipping web search.")
        response["source"] = "local"

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    # STEP 3 — Doc Specialist Agent (optional)
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    if generate_pdf and school_name:
        print(f"\n📋 Step 3: Calling Doc Specialist for '{school_name}'...")
        pdf_result = doc_specialist_agent(
            school_name   = school_name,
            level         = level or "University",
            state         = state or "Texas",
            extra_context = query
        )
        response["agents_called"].append("DocSpecialist")
        response["pdf_result"] = pdf_result
    else:
        print("\n   ℹ️ PDF not requested.")

    print("\n" + "=" * 55)
    print("✅ ORCHESTRATOR COMPLETE")
    print(f"   Agents : {', '.join(response['agents_called'])}")
    print(f"   Source : {response['source']}")
    print("=" * 55)

    return response
Save (Ctrl + S).

Quick Answers First
Point 4 — UT Dallas fee showing $50:
That value comes from our schools.csv where we hardcoded tuition_min=13000. The $50/$75 application fee is a different field we haven't added yet. We'll fix this.
Web Scraping vs Researcher Agent:
Web scraping (BeautifulSoup/Selenium) is fragile — every school website has a different structure, blocks bots, and breaks frequently. Our Researcher Agent already does something better — it uses Tavily which is a live AI-powered search engine that pulls current data from multiple sources in real time. For a capstone this is actually the more impressive and robust approach.
So the answer is — we'll enhance the Researcher Agent to always fetch live fee and rating data to supplement/correct our CSV values.

Let me ask one quick question before coding all changes:While you answer that, here are all the fixes ready to go:

Fix 2, 3 & 4 — Update app.py Sidebar and Logic
Open app.py and replace the entire sidebar section (everything inside with st.sidebar:) with this:
python    with st.sidebar:
        st.markdown(
            '<div class="sidebar-title">🔍 Search Filters</div>',
            unsafe_allow_html=True
        )

        # Step 1: Education Level
        st.markdown("**Step 1 — Education Level**")
        level_options  = ["Select Level"] + get_education_levels()
        selected_level = st.selectbox(
            "Level", options=level_options,
            label_visibility="collapsed"
        )

        # Step 2: State
        st.markdown("**Step 2 — State**")
        state_options  = ["Select State"] + get_all_states()
        selected_state = st.selectbox(
            "State", options=state_options,
            label_visibility="collapsed"
        )

        # Step 3: County (conditional)
        selected_county = None
        county_active   = (
            selected_level != "Select Level" and
            is_county_applicable(selected_level)
        )
        if county_active:
            st.markdown("**Step 3 — County**")
            counties = get_counties_for_level(
                df, selected_state, selected_level
            )
            if counties:
                selected_county = st.selectbox(
                    "County",
                    options=["All Counties"] + counties,
                    label_visibility="collapsed"
                )
            else:
                if selected_state != "Select State":
                    st.info(
                        f"No local {selected_level} data "
                        f"in {selected_state}. "
                        f"AI will search the web."
                    )
        else:
            if selected_level not in ["Select Level"]:
                st.markdown("**Step 3 — County**")
                st.info(f"Not applicable for {selected_level}.")

        st.divider()

        # Search Query + Search Button together
        st.markdown("**💬 What are you looking for?**")
        search_query = st.text_area(
            "Query",
            placeholder=(
                "e.g. best school with STEM programs\n"
                "e.g. UT Austin computer science fees\n"
                "e.g. Montessori with small class sizes\n\n"
                "Press Ctrl+Enter or click Search below"
            ),
            height=120,
            label_visibility="collapsed",
            key="search_query_input"
        )

        # Search button directly below text area
        search_clicked = st.button(
            "🚀 Search with AI",
            use_container_width=True,
            type="primary"
        )

        st.divider()

        # PDF Checklist toggle
        st.markdown("**📄 Generate PDF Checklist**")
        generate_pdf = st.toggle(
            "Generate application checklist PDF",
            value=False
        )
        pdf_school = None
        if generate_pdf:
            pdf_school = st.text_input(
                "School name for checklist",
                placeholder="e.g. UT Austin"
            )

Fix 5 — Update School Card to Show Application Fee
Find the render_school_card function in app.py and replace the chips section with this updated version that includes the application fee:
pythondef render_school_card(row, match_score=None):
    tuition = (
        "Free (Public)"
        if int(row["tuition_min"]) == 0
        else f"${int(row['tuition_min']):,} - ${int(row['tuition_max']):,}/yr"
    )

    # Application fee chip
    app_fee = int(row.get("application_fee", 0))
    fee_chip = (
        '<span class="chip">📋 No App Fee</span>'
        if app_fee == 0
        else f'<span class="chip">📋 App Fee: ${app_fee}</span>'
    )

    ap_chip = (
        f'<span class="chip">📚 {int(row["ap_courses"])} AP</span>'
        if int(row["ap_courses"]) > 0 else ""
    )
    match_html = (
        f'<span class="chip" style="background:#e8f5e9;color:#2e7d32;">'
        f'🎯 Match: {match_score}%</span>'
        if match_score else ""
    )

    card = (
        '<div class="school-card">'
        '<div class="school-name">🏫 ' + str(row["name"]) + '</div>'
        '<div class="school-meta">📍 ' + str(row["city"]) + ', '
            + str(row["county"]) + ' County, ' + str(row["state"])
            + ' &nbsp;|&nbsp; 🏷️ ' + str(row["type"])
            + ' ' + str(row["level"]) + '</div>'
        '<div class="school-desc">' + str(row["description"]) + '</div>'
        + rating_badge(row["rating"]) + '&nbsp;'
        + match_html + '&nbsp;'
        '<span class="chip">💰 ' + tuition + '</span>'
        + fee_chip +
        '<span class="chip">👥 ' + f'{int(row["student_count"]):,}'
            + ' students</span>'
        '<span class="chip">👩‍🏫 ' + str(row["teacher_student_ratio"])
            + '</span>'
        '<span class="chip">🎭 ' + str(int(row["clubs"])) + ' clubs</span>'
        + ap_chip +
        '<div style="margin-top:0.8rem;padding-top:0.8rem;'
            'border-top:1px solid #f0f0f0;font-size:0.8rem;color:#888;">'
            '🗓️ Deadline: ' + str(row["application_deadline"])
            + ' &nbsp;|&nbsp; 🌐 ' + str(row["website"])
        + '</div>'
        '</div>'
    )
    st.markdown(card, unsafe_allow_html=True)

agents/orchestrator.py — Complete File
pythonimport os
import logging
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings("ignore")
logging.getLogger("chromadb").setLevel(logging.ERROR)

from dotenv import load_dotenv
from agents.librarian_agent      import librarian_agent
from agents.researcher_agent     import researcher_agent
from agents.doc_specialist_agent import doc_specialist_agent
from utils.geo_filter            import has_local_data

load_dotenv()

MIN_LOCAL_RESULTS = 2


def orchestrator(
    collection,
    query,
    state        = None,
    level        = None,
    county       = None,
    n_results    = 20,
    generate_pdf = False,
    school_name  = None,
    df           = None
):
    """
    Master Orchestrator — coordinates all three agents.

    Decision Logic:
        1. Check if local DB has data for state + level
        2. If yes  → Librarian Agent (RAG)
        3. If no or insufficient → Researcher Agent (web)
        4. If specific school detected → Researcher Agent
        5. If generate_pdf → Doc Specialist Agent
    """

    print("\n" + "=" * 55)
    print("🎯 ORCHESTRATOR ACTIVATED")
    print(f"   Query  : {query}")
    print(f"   State  : {state}  |  Level : {level}")
    print(f"   County : {county}")
    print("=" * 55)

    response = {
        "source":         None,
        "schools":        [],
        "local_summary":  "",
        "web_summary":    "",
        "web_sources":    [],
        "pdf_result":     None,
        "query":          query,
        "filters_used":   {
            "state":  state,
            "level":  level,
            "county": county
        },
        "agents_called":  [],
        "has_local_data": False
    }

    # ── Build filters for ChromaDB query ──────────
    filters = {}
    if state:
        filters["state"] = state
    if level:
        filters["level"] = level
    if county and county not in ["All Counties", "Select County"]:
        filters["county"] = county

    # ── Check if local DB has data ─────────────────
    local_data_exists = False
    if df is not None and state and level:
        local_data_exists = has_local_data(df, state, level)
    response["has_local_data"] = local_data_exists

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    # STEP 1 — Librarian Agent
    # Only runs when local data exists for
    # the selected state + level combination
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    if local_data_exists:
        print("\n📋 Step 1: Calling Librarian Agent...")
        librarian_result = librarian_agent(
            collection = collection,
            query      = query,
            filters    = filters,
            n_results  = 20
        )
        response["agents_called"].append("Librarian")
        response["schools"]       = librarian_result["schools"]
        response["local_summary"] = librarian_result["summary"]
        local_count               = len(librarian_result["schools"])
        print(f"   📊 Local results: {local_count}")
    else:
        local_count = 0
        print(f"\n   ℹ️ No local data for {level} in {state}.")
        print("      Researcher Agent will handle this.")

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    # STEP 2 — Researcher Agent
    # Triggered when ANY of these are true:
    #   a) No local data for selected state + level
    #   b) Fewer than MIN_LOCAL_RESULTS found
    #   c) Query contains a specific school name
    #   d) User is searching a state with no CSV data
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    specific_keywords = [
        "ut austin", "university of texas austin",
        "harvard", "stanford", "mit", "yale", "princeton",
        "texas tech", "baylor", "rice university",
        "tcu", "texas christian", "duke", "vanderbilt",
        "georgetown", "notre dame", "emory", "tulane",
        "ohio state", "penn state", "purdue", "georgia tech",
        "unc", "unc chapel hill", "virginia tech",
        "university of georgia", "arizona state"
    ]
    query_lower        = query.lower()
    is_specific_school = any(
        kw in query_lower for kw in specific_keywords
    )

    needs_web = (
        not local_data_exists          or
        local_count < MIN_LOCAL_RESULTS or
        is_specific_school
    )

    if needs_web:
        if not local_data_exists:
            reason = f"no local data for {level} in {state}"
        elif is_specific_school:
            reason = "specific school detected in query"
        else:
            reason = f"only {local_count} local results found"

        print(f"\n📋 Step 2: Calling Researcher Agent ({reason})...")
        researcher_result = researcher_agent(
            query     = query,
            state     = state,
            level     = level,
            n_results = 5
        )
        response["agents_called"].append("Researcher")
        response["web_summary"] = researcher_result["summary"]
        response["web_sources"] = researcher_result["sources"]
        response["source"]      = (
            "both" if local_count > 0 else "web"
        )
    else:
        print(f"\n   ✅ Sufficient local data ({local_count} results).")
        print("      Skipping web search.")
        response["source"] = "local"

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    # STEP 3 — Doc Specialist Agent (optional)
    # Only runs when user requests PDF generation
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    if generate_pdf and school_name:
        print(f"\n📋 Step 3: Calling Doc Specialist for '{school_name}'...")
        pdf_result = doc_specialist_agent(
            school_name   = school_name,
            level         = level or "University",
            state         = state or "Texas",
            extra_context = query
        )
        response["agents_called"].append("DocSpecialist")
        response["pdf_result"] = pdf_result
    else:
        print("\n   ℹ️ PDF generation not requested. Skipping.")

    # ── Final Summary ──────────────────────────────
    print("\n" + "=" * 55)
    print("✅ ORCHESTRATOR COMPLETE")
    print(f"   Agents called : {', '.join(response['agents_called'])}")
    print(f"   Source        : {response['source']}")
    print(f"   Local schools : {len(response['schools'])}")
    print(f"   Web sources   : {len(response['web_sources'])}")
    print(f"   PDF generated : {response['pdf_result'] is not None}")
    print("=" * 55)

    return response
Save (Ctrl + S).

app.py — Complete File
pythonimport os
import logging
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings("ignore")
logging.getLogger("chromadb").setLevel(logging.ERROR)

import streamlit as st
from dotenv import load_dotenv
from utils.geo_filter import (
    load_geo_data,
    get_all_states,
    get_education_levels,
    is_county_applicable,
    get_counties_for_level,
    filter_schools,
    get_filter_summary,
    has_local_data
)
from utils.embeddings    import load_vector_db
from agents.orchestrator import orchestrator

load_dotenv()

# ── Page Configuration ─────────────────────────────
st.set_page_config(
    page_title="EduNavigator AI",
    page_icon="🎓",
    layout="wide",
    initial_sidebar_state="expanded"
)

# ── Custom CSS ─────────────────────────────────────
st.markdown("""
<style>
    .main-header {
        background: linear-gradient(135deg, #1e3a5f, #2d6a9f);
        padding: 2rem;
        border-radius: 12px;
        color: white;
        text-align: center;
        margin-bottom: 2rem;
    }
    .main-header h1 {
        font-size: 2.5rem;
        margin: 0;
        font-weight: 700;
    }
    .main-header p {
        font-size: 1.1rem;
        margin: 0.5rem 0 0;
        opacity: 0.9;
    }
    .school-card {
        background: white;
        border: 1px solid #e0e0e0;
        border-radius: 12px;
        padding: 1.2rem;
        margin-bottom: 1rem;

# ── Load Resources Once ────────────────────────────
@st.cache_resource(show_spinner=False)
def get_resources():
    df         = load_geo_data()
    collection = load_vector_db()
    return df, collection


# ── Rating Badge ───────────────────────────────────
def rating_badge(rating):
    r = float(rating)
    if r >= 9.0:
        color, bg, label = "#2e7d32", "#e8f5e9", "Excellent"
    elif r >= 8.0:
        color, bg, label = "#f57f17", "#fff8e1", "Good"
    else:
        color, bg, label = "#c62828", "#fce4ec", "Average"
    return (
        f'<span style="display:inline-block;background:{bg};'
        f'color:{color};border-radius:20px;padding:2px 12px;'
        f'font-size:0.85rem;font-weight:600;">⭐ {label} {r}/10</span>'
    )


# ── School Card ────────────────────────────────────
def render_school_card(row, match_score=None):
    tuition = (
        "Free (Public)"
        if int(row["tuition_min"]) == 0
        else f"${int(row['tuition_min']):,} - ${int(row['tuition_max']):,}/yr"
    )

    app_fee  = int(row.get("application_fee", 0))
    fee_chip = (
        '<span class="chip">📋 No App Fee</span>'
        if app_fee == 0
        else f'<span class="chip">📋 App Fee: ${app_fee}</span>'
    )

    ap_chip = (
        f'<span class="chip">📚 {int(row["ap_courses"])} AP Courses</span>'
        if int(row["ap_courses"]) > 0 else ""
    )

    match_html = (
        f'<span class="chip" style="background:#e8f5e9;color:#2e7d32;">'
        f'🎯 Match: {match_score}%</span>'
        if match_score else ""
    )

    card = (
        '<div class="school-card">'
        '<div class="school-name">🏫 ' + str(row["name"]) + '</div>'
        '<div class="school-meta">'
            '📍 ' + str(row["city"]) + ', '
            + str(row["county"]) + ' County, '
            + str(row["state"])
            + ' &nbsp;|&nbsp; 🏷️ '
            + str(row["type"]) + ' '
            + str(row["level"]) +
        '</div>'
        '<div class="school-desc">' + str(row["description"]) + '</div>'
        + rating_badge(row["rating"]) + '&nbsp;'
        + match_html + '&nbsp;'
        '<span class="chip">💰 ' + tuition + '</span>'
        + fee_chip +
        '<span class="chip">👥 '
            + f'{int(row["student_count"]):,}'
            + ' students</span>'
        '<span class="chip">👩‍🏫 '
            + str(row["teacher_student_ratio"]) + '</span>'
        '<span class="chip">🎭 '
            + str(int(row["clubs"])) + ' clubs</span>'
        + ap_chip +
        '<div style="margin-top:0.8rem;padding-top:0.8rem;'
            'border-top:1px solid #f0f0f0;'
            'font-size:0.8rem;color:#888;">'
            '🗓️ Deadline: ' + str(row["application_deadline"])
            + ' &nbsp;|&nbsp; 🌐 '
            + str(row["website"]) +
        '</div>'
        '</div>'
    )
    st.markdown(card, unsafe_allow_html=True)


# ── Agent Badges ───────────────────────────────────
def render_agent_badges(agents_called):
    badges = {
        "Librarian":    ("badge-librarian",  "📚 Librarian Agent"),
        "Researcher":   ("badge-researcher", "🔍 Researcher Agent"),
        "DocSpecialist":("badge-docspec",    "📄 Doc Specialist")
    }
    html = '<div style="margin-bottom:0.8rem;">'
    html += '<span style="font-size:0.8rem;color:#888;">Agents used: </span>'
    for agent in agents_called:
        if agent in badges:
            css, label = badges[agent]
            html += (
                f'<span class="agent-badge {css}">{label}</span> '
            )
    html += '</div>'
    st.markdown(html, unsafe_allow_html=True)


# ── Main App ───────────────────────────────────────
def main():

    # ── Header ─────────────────────────────────────
    st.markdown("""
    <div class="main-header">
        <h1>🎓 EduNavigator AI</h1>
        <p>Agentic RAG Framework for Hyper-Local Academic Discovery</p>
    </div>
    """, unsafe_allow_html=True)

    # ── Load Resources ─────────────────────────────
    with st.spinner("Initializing EduNavigator AI..."):
        df, collection = get_resources()

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    # SIDEBAR
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    with st.sidebar:
        st.markdown(
            '<div class="sidebar-title">🔍 Search Filters</div>',
            unsafe_allow_html=True
        )

        # ── Step 1: Education Level ────────────────
        st.markdown("**Step 1 — Education Level**")
        level_options  = ["Select Level"] + get_education_levels()
        selected_level = st.selectbox(
            "Level",
            options=level_options,
            label_visibility="collapsed"
        )

        # ── Step 2: State ──────────────────────────
        st.markdown("**Step 2 — State**")
        state_options  = ["Select State"] + get_all_states()
        selected_state = st.selectbox(
            "State",
            options=state_options,
            label_visibility="collapsed"
        )

        # ── Step 3: County (conditional) ──────────
        selected_county = None
        county_active   = (
            selected_level != "Select Level" and
            is_county_applicable(selected_level)
        )

        if county_active:
            st.markdown("**Step 3 — County**")
            counties = get_counties_for_level(
                df, selected_state, selected_level
            )
            if counties:
                selected_county = st.selectbox(
                    "County",
                    options=["All Counties"] + counties,
                    label_visibility="collapsed"
                )
            else:
                if selected_state != "Select State":
                    st.info(
                        f"No local {selected_level} data in "
                        f"{selected_state}. AI Researcher will "
                        f"search the web automatically."
                    )
        else:
            if selected_level not in ["Select Level"]:
                st.markdown("**Step 3 — County**")
                st.info(
                    f"County filter not applicable "
                    f"for {selected_level}."
                )

        st.divider()

        # ── Search Query ───────────────────────────
        st.markdown("**💬 What are you looking for?**")
        search_query = st.text_area(
            "Query",
            placeholder=(
                "e.g. best school with STEM programs\n"
                "e.g. UT Austin computer science fees\n"
                "e.g. Montessori with small class sizes\n\n"
                "Press Ctrl+Enter or click Search below"
            ),
            height=120,
            label_visibility="collapsed",
            key="search_query_input"
        )

        # ── Search Button (directly below query) ──
        search_clicked = st.button(
            "🚀 Search with AI",
            use_container_width=True,
            type="primary"
        )

        st.divider()

        # ── PDF Checklist ──────────────────────────
        st.markdown("**📄 Generate PDF Checklist**")
        generate_pdf = st.toggle(
            "Generate application checklist PDF",
            value=False
        )
        pdf_school = None
        if generate_pdf:
            pdf_school = st.text_input(
                "School name for checklist",
                placeholder="e.g. UT Austin"
            )

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    # MAIN CONTENT
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    filters_ready = (
        selected_level != "Select Level" and
        selected_state != "Select State"
    )

    if not filters_ready:
        # ── Welcome Screen ─────────────────────────
        col1, col2, col3 = st.columns(3)
        with col1:
            st.info(
                "**Step 1**\n\n"
                "Select an education level from "
                "the sidebar to begin."
            )
        with col2:
            st.info(
                "**Step 2**\n\n"
                "Choose your target state."
            )
        with col3:
            st.info(
                "**Step 3**\n\n"
                "For K-12 levels, pick a county "
                "for hyper-local results."
            )

        st.markdown("---")
        st.markdown("### 📊 Platform Overview")
        c1, c2, c3, c4 = st.columns(4)
        c1.metric("Schools in DB",    len(df))
        c2.metric("States Covered",   df["state"].nunique())
        c3.metric("Education Levels", df["level"].nunique())
        c4.metric("Avg Rating",       f"{df['rating'].mean():.1f}/10")

        st.markdown("---")
        st.markdown("### 🤖 How EduNavigator AI Works")
        a1, a2, a3 = st.columns(3)
        with a1:
            st.markdown("""
            **📚 Librarian Agent**

            Searches the local vector database
            using semantic AI matching. Fast and
            precise for schools in our database.
            """)
        with a2:
            st.markdown("""
            **🔍 Researcher Agent**

            Automatically activated when local
            data is missing. Searches the live
            web to find any school anywhere.
            """)
        with a3:
            st.markdown("""
            **📄 Doc Specialist Agent**

            Generates personalized PDF application
            checklists with deadlines, requirements,
            and pro tips for any school.
            """)

    else:
        # ── Filter Summary Banner ──────────────────
        summary = get_filter_summary(
            selected_state,
            selected_level,
            selected_county
        )
        st.markdown(
            f'<div class="filter-banner">📍 {summary}</div>',
            unsafe_allow_html=True
        )

        # ── Check if local data exists ─────────────
        local_exists = has_local_data(
            df, selected_state, selected_level
        )

        # Show web-only banner when no local data
        if not local_exists:
            st.markdown(
                '<div class="web-only-banner">'
                '🌐 No local data found for '
                f'<strong>{selected_level}</strong> in '
                f'<strong>{selected_state}</strong>. '
                'Enter a search query below — the '
                '<strong>Researcher Agent</strong> will '
                'search the web automatically.'
                '</div>',
                unsafe_allow_html=True
            )

        # ══════════════════════════════════════════
        # AI SEARCH MODE
        # Triggered by Search button OR Ctrl+Enter
        # ══════════════════════════════════════════
        if search_clicked and search_query.strip():
            st.markdown(
                f"### 🤖 AI Results for: "
                f"*\"{search_query}\"*"
            )

            with st.spinner("🤖 AI agents working..."):
                result = orchestrator(
                    collection   = collection,
                    query        = search_query,
                    state        = selected_state,
                    level        = selected_level,
                    county       = selected_county,
                    n_results    = 20,
                    generate_pdf = generate_pdf and bool(pdf_school),
                    school_name  = pdf_school,
                    df           = df
                )

            # ── Agent Badges ───────────────────────
            render_agent_badges(result["agents_called"])

            # ── Local Results ──────────────────────
            if result["schools"] and result["local_summary"]:
                st.markdown(
                    '<div class="source-local">'
                    '📚 <strong>Local Database Results</strong>'
                    '</div>',
                    unsafe_allow_html=True
                )

                with st.expander(
                    "📝 AI Analysis", expanded=True
                ):
                    st.markdown(result["local_summary"])

                st.markdown("#### Matching Schools")
                filtered_df = filter_schools(
                    df,
                    state  = selected_state,
                    level  = selected_level,
                    county = selected_county
                )
                for school_meta in result["schools"]:
                    match_row = filtered_df[
                        filtered_df["name"] == school_meta["name"]
                    ]
                    if not match_row.empty:
                        render_school_card(match_row.iloc[0])

            # ── Web Results ────────────────────────
            if result["web_summary"]:
                st.markdown(
                    '<div class="source-web">'
                    '🔍 <strong>Live Web Research Results'
                    '</strong></div>',
                    unsafe_allow_html=True
                )

                with st.expander(
                    "🌐 Web Research Summary", expanded=True
                ):
                    st.markdown(result["web_summary"])

                if result["web_sources"]:
                    st.markdown("#### Sources")
                    for src in result["web_sources"]:
                        st.markdown(
                            f"- [{src['title'][:70]}]"
                            f"({src['url']})"
                        )

            # ── PDF Download ───────────────────────
            if (
                result["pdf_result"] and
                result["pdf_result"]["filepath"]
            ):
                st.markdown("---")
                st.markdown("### 📄 Application Checklist")
                pdf_path = result["pdf_result"]["filepath"]

                col_info, col_btn = st.columns([3, 1])
                with col_info:
                    total = sum(
                        len(v) for v in
                        result["pdf_result"]["checklist"].values()
                    )
                    st.success(
                        f"✅ PDF checklist generated for "
                        f"**{result['pdf_result']['school_name']}"
                        f"** with **{total} items**"
                    )
                with col_btn:
                    with open(pdf_path, "rb") as f:
                        st.download_button(
                            label="📥 Download PDF",
                            data=f,
                            file_name=os.path.basename(pdf_path),
                            mime="application/pdf",
                            use_container_width=True
                        )

                with st.expander(
                    "👀 Preview Checklist", expanded=False
                ):
                    for section, items in (
                        result["pdf_result"]["checklist"].items()
                    ):
                        if items:
                            st.markdown(f"**{section}**")
                            for item in items:
                                st.markdown(f"- ☐ {item}")

            # ── No results at all ──────────────────
            if (
                not result["schools"] and
                not result["web_summary"]
            ):
                st.markdown(
                    '<div class="no-results">'
                    '🔍 No results found.<br>'
                    '<small>Try different keywords '
                    'or adjust your filters.</small>'
                    '</div>',
                    unsafe_allow_html=True
                )

        # ══════════════════════════════════════════
        # BROWSE MODE
        # Shown when no search query entered yet
        # ══════════════════════════════════════════
        else:
            filtered_df = filter_schools(
                df,
                state  = selected_state,
                level  = selected_level,
                county = selected_county
            )

            if len(filtered_df) > 0:
                # Metrics row
                c1, c2, c3, c4 = st.columns(4)
                c1.metric(
                    "Schools Found",
                    len(filtered_df)
                )
                c2.metric(
                    "Avg Rating",
                    f"{filtered_df['rating'].mean():.1f}/10"
                )
                c3.metric(
                    "Top Rated",
                    filtered_df["name"].iloc[
                        filtered_df["rating"].argmax()
                    ]
                )
                c4.metric(
                    "Public Schools",
                    len(filtered_df[
                        filtered_df["type"] == "Public"
                    ])
                )

                st.markdown("---")
                st.markdown(
                    f"### 🏫 {len(filtered_df)} "
                    f"{selected_level} schools "
                    f"in {selected_state}"
                )
                st.caption(
                    "💡 Tip: Enter a search query above "
                    "for AI-powered matching, live web "
                    "research, and smart comparisons."
                )

                # Sort by rating descending
                sorted_df = filtered_df.sort_values(
                    "rating", ascending=False
                ).reset_index(drop=True)

                for _, row in sorted_df.iterrows():
                    render_school_card(row)

            else:
                # No local data — prompt user to search
                st.markdown(
                    '<div class="no-results">'
                    '🔍 No local schools found for these filters.<br>'
                    '<small>Enter a search query above and click '
                    '<strong>Search with AI</strong> — the Researcher '
                    'Agent will find schools from the web.</small>'
                    '</div>',
                    unsafe_allow_html=True
                )


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

Update 1 — agents/orchestrator.py
Find the section that builds the needs_web logic and replace from # ── Check if local DB has data ───────────────── all the way to the end of Step 2, with this:
python    # ── Check if local DB has data ─────────────────
    local_data_exists = False
    if df is not None and state and level:
        local_data_exists = has_local_data(df, state, level)
    response["has_local_data"] = local_data_exists

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    # STEP 1 — Librarian Agent
    # Only runs when local data exists
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    if local_data_exists:
        print("\n📋 Step 1: Calling Librarian Agent...")
        librarian_result = librarian_agent(
            collection = collection,
            query      = query,
            filters    = filters,
            n_results  = 20
        )
        response["agents_called"].append("Librarian")
        response["schools"]       = librarian_result["schools"]
        response["local_summary"] = librarian_result["summary"]
        local_count               = len(librarian_result["schools"])
        print(f"   📊 Local results: {local_count}")
    else:
        local_count = 0
        print(f"\n   ℹ️ No local data for {level} in {state}.")
        print("      Auto-triggering Researcher Agent...")

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    # STEP 2 — Researcher Agent
    # Triggered when ANY of these are true:
    #   a) No local data for selected state + level
    #   b) Fewer than MIN_LOCAL_RESULTS found
    #   c) Query contains a specific school name
    #   d) Auto-query passed from UI for unknown state
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    specific_keywords = [
        "ut austin", "university of texas austin",
        "harvard", "stanford", "mit", "yale", "princeton",
        "texas tech", "baylor", "rice university",
        "tcu", "texas christian", "duke", "vanderbilt",
        "georgetown", "notre dame", "emory", "tulane",
        "ohio state", "penn state", "purdue", "georgia tech",
        "unc", "unc chapel hill", "virginia tech",
        "university of georgia", "arizona state"
    ]
    query_lower        = query.lower()
    is_specific_school = any(
        kw in query_lower for kw in specific_keywords
    )

    # Auto-generated queries from UI always start with
    # "Provide" — always trigger web search for these
    is_auto_query = query.startswith("Provide ")

    needs_web = (
        not local_data_exists           or
        local_count < MIN_LOCAL_RESULTS  or
        is_specific_school               or
        is_auto_query
    )

    if needs_web:
        if is_auto_query:
            reason = "auto-triggered — no local data found"
        elif not local_data_exists:
            reason = f"no local data for {level} in {state}"
        elif is_specific_school:
            reason = "specific school detected in query"
        else:
            reason = f"only {local_count} local results"

        print(f"\n📋 Step 2: Calling Researcher Agent ({reason})...")
        researcher_result = researcher_agent(
            query     = query,
            state     = state,
            level     = level,
            n_results = 5
        )
        response["agents_called"].append("Researcher")
        response["web_summary"] = researcher_result["summary"]
        response["web_sources"] = researcher_result["sources"]
        response["source"]      = (
            "both" if local_count > 0 else "web"
        )
    else:
        print(f"\n   ✅ Sufficient local data ({local_count} results).")
        response["source"] = "local"
Save (Ctrl + S).

                    ]
                )
                c4.metric(
                    "Public Schools",
                    len(filtered_df[
                        filtered_df["type"] == "Public"
                    ])
                )

                st.markdown("---")
                st.markdown(
                    f"### 🏫 {len(filtered_df)} "
                    f"{selected_level} schools "
                    f"in {selected_state}"
                )
                st.caption(
                    "💡 Tip: Enter a search query above "
                    "for AI-powered matching, live web "
                    "research, and smart comparisons."
                )

                sorted_df = filtered_df.sort_values(
                    "rating", ascending=False
                ).reset_index(drop=True)
                for _, row in sorted_df.iterrows():
                    render_school_card(row)

            else:
                # ── No local data — auto web search ─
                auto_query = (
                    f"Provide {selected_level} "
                    f"data in {selected_state}"
                )

                st.markdown(
                    '<div class="web-only-banner">'
                    f'🌐 No local data found for '
                    f'<strong>{selected_level}</strong> in '
                    f'<strong>{selected_state}</strong>. '
                    f'Activating <strong>Researcher Agent'
                    f'</strong> automatically...'
                    '</div>',
                    unsafe_allow_html=True
                )

                st.markdown(
                    f"### 🤖 Auto Search: *\"{auto_query}\"*"
                )

                with st.spinner(
                    f"🔍 Searching web for "
                    f"{selected_level} schools "
                    f"in {selected_state}..."
                ):
                    result = orchestrator(
                        collection   = collection,
                        query        = auto_query,
                        state        = selected_state,
                        level        = selected_level,
                        county       = selected_county,
                        n_results    = 20,
                        generate_pdf = False,
                        school_name  = None,
                        df           = df
                    )

                # Show agent badges
                render_agent_badges(result["agents_called"])

                # Show web results
                if result["web_summary"]:
                    st.markdown(
                        '<div class="source-web">'
                        '🔍 <strong>Live Web Research Results'
                        '</strong></div>',
                        unsafe_allow_html=True
                    )
                    with st.expander(
                        "🌐 Web Research Summary",
                        expanded=True
                    ):
                        st.markdown(result["web_summary"])

                    if result["web_sources"]:
                        st.markdown("#### Sources")
                        for src in result["web_sources"]:
                            st.markdown(
                                f"- [{src['title'][:70]}]"
                                f"({src['url']})"
                            )

                    # Prompt user to refine search
                    st.info(
                        "💡 Use the search box above to ask "
                        "more specific questions about these "
                        "schools — e.g. fees, admission "
                        "requirements, rankings."
                    )

                elif not result["web_summary"]:
                    st.warning(
                        f"No results found for "
                        f"{selected_level} in "
                        f"{selected_state}. "
                        f"Try a different state or "
                        f"enter a specific school name "
                        f"in the search box."
                    )
Save (Ctrl + S).

Let me know when you're ready to continue with the remaining app improvements or need a presentation slide deck! 🎓Edunavigator ai technical approachDocument · DOCX Downloadprovide me the short description of the technical approach below 200 wordsApr 2EduNavigator AI is an intelligent educational discovery platform built on an Agentic Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) architecture. It helps students and parents find schools and universities across all 50 U.S. states — from preschools to graduate programs — through a coordinated multi-agent AI system.
The platform solves three critical problems: information fragmentation, outdated static data, and zero personalization in existing school search tools.
Three specialized AI agents work under a central Orchestrator:

Librarian Agent performs semantic search on a local ChromaDB vector database using sentence-transformer embeddings and Groq LLaMA 3.3 70B for intelligent school comparison.
Researcher Agent automatically activates when local data is unavailable, using Tavily API to retrieve live, current school data from the web in real time.
Document Specialist Agent generates personalized PDF application checklists with deadlines, requirements, and pro tips tailored to each school.

A smart geographic filter implements context-aware cascading selection — universities filter at state level while K-12 schools support hyper-local county-level search.
The entire stack is 100% free — Groq (LLM), ChromaDB (vector DB), sentence-transformers (embeddings), and Tavily (web search) — making it fully reproducible without any paid services.Provide the tools, libraries, and models used -

Let me research the best approach thoroughly before recommending.Searched the webSearched the webGreat research done. Here is my thorough analysis and recommendation:

My Recommendation — Hybrid Architecture (Best of Both Worlds)
Neither of your two options alone is the right answer. Here's why, and what I recommend instead:

Why Option 1 (Full CSV Dataset) Won't Work Well
Storing all US schools in a CSV file means:

100,000+ K-12 public schools in the US (per NCES data)
6,000+ colleges and universities (per IPEDS)
Medical schools, law schools, trade schools — thousands more
Total records would exceed 150,000+ rows
ChromaDB embedding all of these on a laptop would take hours and consume 10+ GB RAM
Data goes stale immediately — fees, ratings, and deadlines change every year
Maintaining the CSV manually is impossible


Why Option 2 (Skip Database, Web Only) Won't Work Well
Going fully web-search based means:

Every single query hits Tavily — 1000 searches/month free limit exhausted in days
Search results are unstructured text — hard to display as clean cards with chips
No semantic similarity ranking — just keyword matching
Slow — every browse action waits for web results
No offline capability


The Smart Hybrid Solution — 3 Official Free Government APIs
After research, I found three free, official US Government APIs that together cover every education level perfectly:

The Three APIs That Solve Everything
API 1 — College Scorecard (Universities, Colleges, Medical Schools)
The College Scorecard API provides access to data about US higher education institutions including costs, graduation rates, admissions, and programs. It filters by state, city, school name, and much more. College Scorecard
The dataset includes Doctoral/Research Universities, Masters Colleges, Baccalaureate Colleges, Associates Colleges, Theological seminaries, Medical Schools and other health care professions, Schools of engineering and technology, business and management, art, music, design, Law schools, Teachers colleges, Tribal colleges, and other specialized institutions covering all 50 states. Opendatasoft

Free API key: https://api.data.gov/signup
Covers: Universities, Community Colleges, Medical Schools, Law Schools, Trade Schools
Data fields: name, state, city, tuition (in-state/out-of-state), acceptance rate, student size, programs offered


API 2 — NCES Common Core of Data (All K-12 Public Schools)
The Common Core of Data (CCD) is the Department of Education's primary database on public elementary and secondary education. It is a comprehensive, annual, national database of all public elementary and secondary schools and school districts. NCES
The 2024-25 preliminary directory files include basic identifying information for each public school including NCES identification numbers, location, mailing address, type, operational status, the lowest and highest grades offered, and whether a school is a charter school. NCES Kids' Zone

Free — no API key needed
Covers: All public Preschool, Elementary, Middle School, High Schools across all 50 states
Data fields: name, state, county, city, grade range, school type, charter status


API 3 — Urban Institute Education Data API (Enriched Data)
The Education Data Portal datasets include the US Department of Education Common Core of Data, Civil Rights Data Collection, US Census Bureau Small Area Income and Poverty Estimates, IPEDS, and College Scorecard — accessible via a unified API in Python, R, Stata, and JavaScript. Urban

Free — no key needed
Covers: Enrollment, demographics, staff ratios, test scores
Best for: enriching K-12 records with student counts and teacher ratios


Revised Architecture Plan
EduNavigator AI — Phase 7 (Upgraded Data Layer)
│
├── For Universities/Colleges/Medical Schools
│   └── College Scorecard API (live, real-time)
│       → Filter by state, school type, programs
│       → Returns: name, tuition, city, acceptance rate
│
├── For K-12 (Elementary, Middle, High School, Preschool)
│   └── NCES CCD API (live, real-time)
│       → Filter by state, county, grade level
│       → Returns: name, address, type, grades
│
├── For Enrichment (ratings, fees, current info)
│   └── Researcher Agent (Tavily) — still used
│       → Called only for specific school deep-dives
│       → Saves Tavily quota for quality queries
│
└── ChromaDB — Cache Layer
    → Store API results locally after first query
    → Same state+level = instant results on repeat
    → No re-fetching unless user clears cache

How Medical Schools Get Covered
Medical schools are classified as higher education institutions under IPEDS. The College Scorecard/IPEDS dataset explicitly includes Medical Schools and other health care professions institutions. Opendatasoft We just need to add Medical School as a new education level in our dropdown and query the College Scorecard API filtering by school.degrees_awarded.predominant=4 (graduate level) and filter results by program name containing "medicine" or "health".
