Phase 7 — Step 2: Build College Scorecard API Utility
Create utils/college_scorecard_api.py and paste this:
pythonimport os
import requests
import logging
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings("ignore")
logging.getLogger("chromadb").setLevel(logging.ERROR)

from dotenv import load_dotenv
load_dotenv()

SCORECARD_API_KEY = os.getenv("COLLEGE_SCORECARD_API_KEY")
SCORECARD_BASE    = "https://api.data.gov/ed/collegescorecard/v1/schools"

# Mapping our education levels to College Scorecard degree types
LEVEL_TO_DEGREE = {
    "University":        4,   # Bachelor's and above
    "Community College": 2,   # Associate's
    "Medical School":    4,   # Graduate / professional
}

# School type filter for medical schools
MEDICAL_KEYWORDS = [
    "medicine", "medical", "health sciences",
    "pharmacy", "nursing", "dental", "osteopathic",
    "chiropractic", "optometry", "veterinary"
]


def get_state_abbreviation(state_name):
    """Convert full state name to 2-letter abbreviation."""
    states = {
        "Alabama": "AL", "Alaska": "AK", "Arizona": "AZ",
        "Arkansas": "AR", "California": "CA", "Colorado": "CO",
        "Connecticut": "CT", "Delaware": "DE", "Florida": "FL",
        "Georgia": "GA", "Hawaii": "HI", "Idaho": "ID",
        "Illinois": "IL", "Indiana": "IN", "Iowa": "IA",
        "Kansas": "KS", "Kentucky": "KY", "Louisiana": "LA",
        "Maine": "ME", "Maryland": "MD", "Massachusetts": "MA",
        "Michigan": "MI", "Minnesota": "MN", "Mississippi": "MS",
        "Missouri": "MO", "Montana": "MT", "Nebraska": "NE",
        "Nevada": "NV", "New Hampshire": "NH", "New Jersey": "NJ",
        "New Mexico": "NM", "New York": "NY", "North Carolina": "NC",
        "North Dakota": "ND", "Ohio": "OH", "Oklahoma": "OK",
        "Oregon": "OR", "Pennsylvania": "PA", "Rhode Island": "RI",
        "South Carolina": "SC", "South Dakota": "SD",
        "Tennessee": "TN", "Texas": "TX", "Utah": "UT",
        "Vermont": "VT", "Virginia": "VA", "Washington": "WA",
        "West Virginia": "WV", "Wisconsin": "WI", "Wyoming": "WY"
    }
    return states.get(state_name, state_name)


def fetch_universities(state, level="University", per_page=20):
    """
    Fetch universities, community colleges, or medical schools
    from the College Scorecard API for a given state.

    Returns list of standardized school dicts.
    """
    print(f"\n🎓 College Scorecard API: Fetching {level} in {state}...")

    state_abbr = get_state_abbreviation(state)
    degree     = LEVEL_TO_DEGREE.get(level, 4)

    # Build fields to retrieve
    fields = ",".join([
        "school.name",
        "school.city",
        "school.state",
        "school.school_url",
        "school.ownership",
        "school.locale",
        "latest.cost.tuition.in_state",
        "latest.cost.tuition.out_of_state",
        "latest.student.size",
        "latest.admissions.admission_rate.overall",
        "latest.admissions.sat_scores.average.overall",
        "latest.completion.rate_suppressed.overall",
        "school.degrees_awarded.predominant",
        "school.carnegie_basic",
        "latest.programs.cip_4_digit",
        "school.zip",
    ])

    params = {
        "api_key":       SCORECARD_API_KEY,
        "school.state":  state_abbr,
        "fields":        fields,
        "per_page":      per_page,
        "_sort":         "latest.student.size:desc",
    }

    # Filter by degree level
    if level == "Community College":
        params["school.degrees_awarded.predominant"] = 2
    elif level in ["University", "Medical School"]:
        params["school.degrees_awarded.predominant__range"] = "3..4"

    try:
        response = requests.get(
            SCORECARD_BASE, params=params, timeout=15
        )
        response.raise_for_status()
        data = response.json()
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ❌ API error: {e}")
        return []

    results  = data.get("results", [])
    schools  = []

    for r in results:
        name = r.get("school.name", "Unknown")

        # Filter medical schools by name keyword
        if level == "Medical School":
            name_lower = name.lower()
            if not any(kw in name_lower for kw in MEDICAL_KEYWORDS):
                continue

        # Ownership type
        ownership = r.get("school.ownership", 0)
        school_type = (
            "Public"  if ownership == 1 else
            "Private" if ownership in [2, 3] else
            "Unknown"
        )

        # Tuition
        tuition_in  = r.get("latest.cost.tuition.in_state")  or 0
        tuition_out = r.get("latest.cost.tuition.out_of_state") or 0
        tuition_min = min(tuition_in, tuition_out) if tuition_in and tuition_out else max(tuition_in, tuition_out)
        tuition_max = max(tuition_in, tuition_out)

        # Admission rate
        admit_rate = r.get("latest.admissions.admission_rate.overall")
        admit_text = (
            f"{round(admit_rate * 100, 1)}% acceptance rate"
            if admit_rate else "Acceptance rate not reported"
        )

        # Student size
        student_size = r.get("latest.student.size") or 0

        # Build description
        completion = r.get("latest.completion.rate_suppressed.overall")
        completion_text = (
            f" Graduation rate: {round(completion * 100, 1)}%."
            if completion else ""
        )
        description = (
            f"{school_type} {level} in {r.get('school.city', '')}, "
            f"{state}. {admit_text}.{completion_text}"
        )

        website = r.get("school.school_url") or ""
        if website and not website.startswith("http"):
            website = "https://" + website

        school = {
            "school_id":             f"API_{state_abbr}_{name[:10].replace(' ','_')}",
            "name":                   name,
            "type":                   school_type,
            "level":                  level,
            "state":                  state,
            "county":                 "",
            "city":                   r.get("school.city", ""),
            "rating":                 round(min(9.9, 7.0 + (
                                        (1 - (admit_rate or 0.5)) * 3
                                      )), 1),
            "tuition_min":            int(tuition_min),
            "tuition_max":            int(tuition_max),
            "student_count":          int(student_size),
            "teacher_student_ratio":  "N/A",
            "ap_courses":             0,
            "clubs":                  0,
            "application_deadline":   "Check website",
            "website":                website,
            "application_fee":        0,
            "description":            description,
            "source":                 "College Scorecard API"
        }
        schools.append(school)

    print(f"   ✅ Retrieved {len(schools)} {level} institutions.")
    return schools
Save (Ctrl + S).

Phase 7 — Step 3: Build NCES K-12 API Utility
Create utils/nces_api.py and paste this:
pythonimport requests
import logging
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings("ignore")
logging.getLogger("chromadb").setLevel(logging.ERROR)

# Urban Institute Education Data API — no key required
URBAN_BASE = "https://educationdata.urban.org/api/v1"

# NCES grade range mapping for each education level
LEVEL_TO_GRADES = {
    "Preschool":   {"low": "PK", "high": "PK"},
    "Elementary":  {"low": "KG", "high": "06"},
    "Middle School":{"low": "06","high": "08"},
    "High School": {"low": "09", "high": "12"},
}

# FIPS state codes
STATE_FIPS = {
    "Alabama": "01", "Alaska": "02", "Arizona": "04",
    "Arkansas": "05", "California": "06", "Colorado": "08",
    "Connecticut": "09", "Delaware": "10", "Florida": "12",
    "Georgia": "13", "Hawaii": "15", "Idaho": "16",
    "Illinois": "17", "Indiana": "18", "Iowa": "19",
    "Kansas": "20", "Kentucky": "21", "Louisiana": "22",
    "Maine": "23", "Maryland": "24", "Massachusetts": "25",
    "Michigan": "26", "Minnesota": "27", "Mississippi": "28",
    "Missouri": "29", "Montana": "30", "Nebraska": "31",
    "Nevada": "32", "New Hampshire": "33", "New Jersey": "34",
    "New Mexico": "35", "New York": "36", "North Carolina": "37",
    "North Dakota": "38", "Ohio": "39", "Oklahoma": "40",
    "Oregon": "41", "Pennsylvania": "42", "Rhode Island": "44",
    "South Carolina": "45", "South Dakota": "46",
    "Tennessee": "47", "Texas": "48", "Utah": "49",
    "Vermont": "50", "Virginia": "51", "Washington": "53",
    "West Virginia": "54", "Wisconsin": "55", "Wyoming": "56"
}


def fetch_k12_schools(state, level, county=None, limit=30):
    """
    Fetch K-12 schools from the Urban Institute / NCES CCD API.
    No API key required.

    Returns list of standardized school dicts.
    """
    print(f"\n🏫 NCES API: Fetching {level} schools in {state}...")

    fips = STATE_FIPS.get(state)
    if not fips:
        print(f"   ❌ State FIPS not found for {state}")
        return []

    grade_map  = LEVEL_TO_GRADES.get(level, {})
    grade_low  = grade_map.get("low",  "KG")
    grade_high = grade_map.get("high", "12")

    # Query CCD school directory
    url    = f"{URBAN_BASE}/schools/ccd/directory/2022/"
    params = {
        "fips":        fips,
        "grade_low":   grade_low,
        "grade_high":  grade_high,
        "per_page":    limit,
        "page":        1,
    }

    try:
        response = requests.get(url, params=params, timeout=20)
        response.raise_for_status()
        data = response.json()
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ❌ NCES API error: {e}")
        return []

    results = data.get("results", [])
    schools = []

    for r in results:
        name = r.get("school_name", "Unknown School")
        city = r.get("city_location", "")
        cty  = r.get("county_name", county or "")

        # Skip if county filter applied and doesn't match
        if county and county not in ["All Counties", "Select County"]:
            if cty and county.lower() not in cty.lower():
                continue

        # School type
        charter    = r.get("charter", 0)
        magnet     = r.get("magnet", 0)
        school_type = (
            "Charter" if charter == 1 else
            "Magnet"  if magnet  == 1 else
            "Public"
        )

        # Build description
        low_grade  = r.get("lowest_grade_offered",  grade_low)
        high_grade = r.get("highest_grade_offered", grade_high)
        description = (
            f"{school_type} {level} school in {city}, {state}. "
            f"Grades {low_grade} through {high_grade}. "
            f"Operated by {r.get('lea_name', 'local school district')}."
        )

        school = {
            "school_id":             f"NCES_{r.get('ncessch', name[:8])}",
            "name":                   name,
            "type":                   school_type,
            "level":                  level,
            "state":                  state,
            "county":                 cty,
            "city":                   city,
            "rating":                 0.0,
            "tuition_min":            0,
            "tuition_max":            0,
            "student_count":          int(r.get("enrollment", 0) or 0),
            "teacher_student_ratio":  "N/A",
            "ap_courses":             0,
            "clubs":                  0,
            "application_deadline":   "Contact school",
            "website":                r.get("website", ""),
            "application_fee":        0,
            "description":            description,
            "source":                 "NCES CCD API"
        }
        schools.append(school)

    print(f"   ✅ Retrieved {len(schools)} {level} schools.")
    return schools

Phase 7 — Step 4: Update get_education_levels in geo_filter.py

Phase 7 — Step 5: Update the Orchestrator
Open agents/orchestrator.py and replace the entire file with this:
pythonimport os
import logging
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings("ignore")
logging.getLogger("chromadb").setLevel(logging.ERROR)

from dotenv import load_dotenv
from agents.librarian_agent      import librarian_agent
from agents.researcher_agent     import researcher_agent
from agents.doc_specialist_agent import doc_specialist_agent
from utils.geo_filter            import has_local_data
from utils.college_scorecard_api import fetch_universities
from utils.nces_api              import fetch_k12_schools

load_dotenv()

MIN_LOCAL_RESULTS = 2

K12_LEVELS  = ["Preschool", "Elementary", "Middle School", "High School"]
UNI_LEVELS  = ["University", "Community College", "Medical School"]


def orchestrator(
    collection,
    query,
    state        = None,
    level        = None,
    county       = None,
    n_results    = 20,
    generate_pdf = False,
    school_name  = None,
    df           = None
):
    print("\n" + "=" * 55)
    print("🎯 ORCHESTRATOR ACTIVATED")
    print(f"   Query  : {query}")
    print(f"   State  : {state}  |  Level : {level}")
    print(f"   County : {county}")
    print("=" * 55)

    response = {
        "source":          None,
        "schools":         [],
        "api_schools":     [],
        "local_summary":   "",
        "web_summary":     "",
        "web_sources":     [],
        "pdf_result":      None,
        "query":           query,
        "filters_used":    {
            "state": state, "level": level, "county": county
        },
        "agents_called":   [],
        "has_local_data":  False
    }

    filters = {}
    if state:
        filters["state"] = state
    if level:
        filters["level"] = level
    if county and county not in ["All Counties", "Select County"]:
        filters["county"] = county

    # ── Check local CSV data ───────────────────────
    local_data_exists = False
    if df is not None and state and level:
        local_data_exists = has_local_data(df, state, level)
    response["has_local_data"] = local_data_exists

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    # STEP 1 — Librarian Agent (local CSV data)
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    if local_data_exists:
        print("\n📋 Step 1: Calling Librarian Agent (local data)...")
        librarian_result = librarian_agent(
            collection = collection,
            query      = query,
            filters    = filters,
            n_results  = 20
        )
        response["agents_called"].append("Librarian")
        response["schools"]      = librarian_result["schools"]
        response["local_summary"]= librarian_result["summary"]
        local_count              = len(librarian_result["schools"])
        print(f"   📊 Local results: {local_count}")
    else:
        local_count = 0
        print(f"\n   ℹ️ No local CSV data for {level} in {state}.")

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    # STEP 2 — Government API Fetch
    # For University/College/Medical → College Scorecard
    # For K-12 → NCES CCD API
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    api_schools = []

    if not local_data_exists and state and level:
        if level in UNI_LEVELS:
            print(f"\n📋 Step 2: Calling College Scorecard API for {level} in {state}...")
            api_schools = fetch_universities(
                state=state, level=level, per_page=20
            )
            response["agents_called"].append("CollegeScorecard")

        elif level in K12_LEVELS:
            print(f"\n📋 Step 2: Calling NCES CCD API for {level} in {state}...")
            api_schools = fetch_k12_schools(
                state=state, level=level,
                county=county, limit=30
            )
            response["agents_called"].append("NCES_API")

        response["api_schools"] = api_schools
        if api_schools:
            response["source"] = "api"
            print(f"   ✅ API returned {len(api_schools)} schools.")
        else:
            print("   ⚠️ API returned no results. Falling back to web search.")

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    # STEP 3 — Researcher Agent (web search)
    # Triggered when:
    #   a) API returned no results
    #   b) Query has specific school name
    #   c) Auto-generated "Provide X in Y" query
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    specific_keywords = [
        "ut austin", "harvard", "stanford", "mit", "yale",
        "princeton", "texas tech", "baylor", "rice university",
        "tcu", "duke", "vanderbilt", "georgetown", "notre dame",
        "emory", "tulane", "ohio state", "penn state", "purdue",
        "georgia tech", "virginia tech", "arizona state"
    ]
    query_lower        = query.lower()
    is_specific_school = any(
        kw in query_lower for kw in specific_keywords
    )
    is_auto_query      = query.startswith("Provide ")

    needs_web = (
        (not local_data_exists and not api_schools) or
        is_specific_school                           or
        is_auto_query
    )

    if needs_web:
        if is_specific_school:
            reason = "specific school query detected"
        elif not api_schools:
            reason = "API returned no results — falling back"
        else:
            reason = "auto-triggered query"

        print(f"\n📋 Step 3: Calling Researcher Agent ({reason})...")
        researcher_result = researcher_agent(
            query     = query,
            state     = state,
            level     = level,
            n_results = 5
        )
        response["agents_called"].append("Researcher")
        response["web_summary"] = researcher_result["summary"]
        response["web_sources"] = researcher_result["sources"]

        if local_count > 0 or api_schools:
            response["source"] = "both"
        else:
            response["source"] = "web"
    else:
        if local_count > 0:
            response["source"] = "local"

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    # STEP 4 — Doc Specialist Agent (PDF)
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    if generate_pdf and school_name:
        print(f"\n📋 Step 4: Doc Specialist for '{school_name}'...")
        pdf_result = doc_specialist_agent(
            school_name   = school_name,
            level         = level or "University",
            state         = state or "Texas",
            extra_context = query
        )
        response["agents_called"].append("DocSpecialist")
        response["pdf_result"] = pdf_result
    else:
        print("\n   ℹ️ PDF not requested.")

    print("\n" + "=" * 55)
    print("✅ ORCHESTRATOR COMPLETE")
    print(f"   Agents  : {', '.join(response['agents_called'])}")
    print(f"   Source  : {response['source']}")
    print(f"   Local   : {len(response['schools'])}")
    print(f"   API     : {len(response['api_schools'])}")
    print(f"   Web src : {len(response['web_sources'])}")
    print("=" * 55)

    return response
Save (Ctrl + S).

Phase 7 — Step 6: Update app.py to Display API Results
Find the render_school_card function in app.py and add this new function right after it:
pythondef render_api_school_card(school):
    """
    Render a school card for API-sourced data
    (College Scorecard or NCES CCD).
    """
    tuition = (
        "Free / Public"
        if int(school.get("tuition_min", 0)) == 0
        else f"${int(school['tuition_min']):,} - "
             f"${int(school['tuition_max']):,}/yr"
    )

    student_count = int(school.get("student_count", 0))
    students_text = (
        f"{student_count:,} students"
        if student_count > 0 else "Size not reported"
    )

    source_badge = (
        '<span style="background:#e3f2fd;color:#1565c0;'
        'border-radius:20px;padding:2px 10px;'
        'font-size:0.75rem;font-weight:600;">'
        '🏛️ ' + school.get("source", "API") + '</span>'
    )

    website = school.get("website", "")
    website_html = (
        f'<a href="{website}" target="_blank" '
        f'style="color:#1565c0;">{website[:50]}</a>'
        if website else "Website not available"
    )

    card = (
        '<div class="school-card">'
        '<div class="school-name">🏫 '
            + str(school["name"]) + '</div>'
        '<div class="school-meta">'
            '📍 ' + str(school.get("city", "")) + ', '
            + str(school.get("state", ""))
            + ' &nbsp;|&nbsp; 🏷️ '
            + str(school.get("type", "")) + ' '
            + str(school.get("level", "")) +
        '</div>'
        '<div class="school-desc">'
            + str(school.get("description", "")) +
        '</div>'
        + source_badge + '&nbsp;'
        '<span class="chip">💰 ' + tuition + '</span>'
        '<span class="chip">👥 ' + students_text + '</span>'
        '<div style="margin-top:0.8rem;padding-top:0.8rem;'
            'border-top:1px solid #f0f0f0;'
            'font-size:0.8rem;color:#888;">'
            '🗓️ Deadline: '
            + str(school.get("application_deadline", "Check website"))
            + ' &nbsp;|&nbsp; 🌐 '
            + website_html +
        '</div>'
        '</div>'
    )
    st.markdown(card, unsafe_allow_html=True)

Fix 2 — Replace NCES API with NCES EDGE API
The Urban Institute API times out frequently. Replace the entire utils/nces_api.py with this version that uses the official NCES EDGE ArcGIS API which is faster and more reliable:
pythonimport requests
import logging
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings("ignore")
logging.getLogger("chromadb").setLevel(logging.ERROR)

# NCES EDGE ArcGIS REST API — official, no key required, faster
NCES_EDGE_BASE = (
    "https://nces.ed.gov/opengis/rest/services/K-12_School_Locations"
    "/EDGE_GEOCODE_PUBLICSCH_2324/MapServer/0/query"
)

# Grade range mapping per education level
LEVEL_TO_GRADES = {
    "Preschool":    ("PK", "PK"),
    "Elementary":   ("KG", "06"),
    "Middle School":("06", "08"),
    "High School":  ("09", "12"),
}

# State abbreviations
STATE_ABBR = {
    "Alabama": "AL", "Alaska": "AK", "Arizona": "AZ",
    "Arkansas": "AR", "California": "CA", "Colorado": "CO",
    "Connecticut": "CT", "Delaware": "DE", "Florida": "FL",
    "Georgia": "GA", "Hawaii": "HI", "Idaho": "ID",
    "Illinois": "IL", "Indiana": "IN", "Iowa": "IA",
    "Kansas": "KS", "Kentucky": "KY", "Louisiana": "LA",
    "Maine": "ME", "Maryland": "MD", "Massachusetts": "MA",
    "Michigan": "MI", "Minnesota": "MN", "Mississippi": "MS",
    "Missouri": "MO", "Montana": "MT", "Nebraska": "NE",
    "Nevada": "NV", "New Hampshire": "NH", "New Jersey": "NJ",
    "New Mexico": "NM", "New York": "NY", "North Carolina": "NC",
    "North Dakota": "ND", "Ohio": "OH", "Oklahoma": "OK",
    "Oregon": "OR", "Pennsylvania": "PA", "Rhode Island": "RI",
    "South Carolina": "SC", "South Dakota": "SD",
    "Tennessee": "TN", "Texas": "TX", "Utah": "UT",
    "Vermont": "VT", "Virginia": "VA", "Washington": "WA",
    "West Virginia": "WV", "Wisconsin": "WI", "Wyoming": "WY"
}

# School level codes in NCES data
LEVEL_CODES = {
    "Preschool":    ["1"],           # Primary with PK
    "Elementary":   ["1", "2"],      # Primary, Elementary
    "Middle School":["3"],           # Middle
    "High School":  ["4", "5"],      # High, Secondary
}


def fetch_k12_schools(state, level, county=None, limit=30):
    """
    Fetch K-12 schools from the official NCES EDGE ArcGIS API.
    No API key required. Fast and reliable.

    Returns list of standardized school dicts.
    """
    print(f"\n🏫 NCES EDGE API: Fetching {level} schools in {state}...")

    state_abbr = STATE_ABBR.get(state)
    if not state_abbr:
        print(f"   ❌ State abbreviation not found for {state}")
        return []

    level_codes = LEVEL_CODES.get(level, ["1", "2", "3", "4"])

    # Build SQL WHERE clause
    level_filter = " OR ".join(
        [f"SCHLEVEL='{c}'" for c in level_codes]
    )
    where_clause = (
        f"STATE='{state_abbr}' AND ({level_filter}) "
        f"AND STATUS='1'"  # Active schools only
    )

    # Add county filter if provided
    if county and county not in ["All Counties", "Select County"]:
        # NCES uses county name — try partial match
        county_clean = county.replace(" County", "").strip()
        where_clause += f" AND UPPER(NMCNTY) LIKE UPPER('%{county_clean}%')"

    params = {
        "where":        where_clause,
        "outFields":    (
            "NAME,CITY,STATE,NMCNTY,STNAME,"
            "SCHLEVEL,CHARTER,MAGNET,LOCALE,"
            "ULOCALE,WEBSITE,NCESSCH,SURVYEAR"
        ),
        "returnGeometry": "false",
        "resultRecordCount": limit,
        "orderByFields": "NAME ASC",
        "f":            "json",
    }

    try:
        response = requests.get(
            NCES_EDGE_BASE,
            params=params,
            timeout=30
        )
        response.raise_for_status()
        data = response.json()
    except requests.exceptions.Timeout:
        print("   ⚠️ NCES EDGE API timed out. Trying fallback...")
        return _fetch_k12_fallback(state, level, county, limit)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ❌ NCES EDGE API error: {e}")
        return _fetch_k12_fallback(state, level, county, limit)

    features = data.get("features", [])
    if not features:
        print("   ⚠️ No results from NCES EDGE. Trying fallback...")
        return _fetch_k12_fallback(state, level, county, limit)

    schools = []
    for feat in features:
        attr = feat.get("attributes", {})
        name = attr.get("NAME", "Unknown School")
        city = attr.get("CITY", "")
        cty  = attr.get("NMCNTY", county or "")

        # School type
        charter = attr.get("CHARTER", "")
        magnet  = attr.get("MAGNET",  "")
        school_type = (
            "Charter" if charter == "Y" else
            "Magnet"  if magnet  == "Y" else
            "Public"
        )

        # Locale description
        locale_map = {
            "11": "City: Large", "12": "City: Midsize",
            "13": "City: Small", "21": "Suburb: Large",
            "22": "Suburb: Midsize", "31": "Town: Fringe",
            "41": "Rural: Fringe", "42": "Rural: Distant",
            "43": "Rural: Remote",
        }
        locale_code = str(attr.get("ULOCALE", ""))
        locale_text = locale_map.get(locale_code, "")

        description = (
            f"{school_type} {level} school in "
            f"{city}, {attr.get('STNAME', state)}. "
            f"{locale_text + '. ' if locale_text else ''}"
            f"County: {cty}."
        )

        website = attr.get("WEBSITE", "") or ""
        if website and not website.startswith("http"):
            website = "https://" + website

        schools.append({
            "school_id":            f"NCES_{attr.get('NCESSCH', name[:8])}",
            "name":                  name,
            "type":                  school_type,
            "level":                 level,
            "state":                 state,
            "county":                cty,
            "city":                  city,
            "rating":                0.0,
            "tuition_min":           0,
            "tuition_max":           0,
            "student_count":         0,
            "teacher_student_ratio": "N/A",
            "ap_courses":            0,
            "clubs":                 0,
            "application_deadline":  "Contact school",
            "website":               website,
            "application_fee":       0,
            "description":           description,
            "source":               "NCES EDGE API"
        })

    print(f"   ✅ Retrieved {len(schools)} {level} schools.")
    return schools


def _fetch_k12_fallback(state, level, county, limit):
    """
    Fallback using OpenDataSoft NCES public schools API.
    Used when NCES EDGE times out.
    """
    print(f"   🔄 Fallback: OpenDataSoft NCES API...")

    state_abbr = STATE_ABBR.get(state, state)
    url        = (
        "https://public.opendatasoft.com/api/explore/v2.1"
        "/catalog/datasets/us-public-schools/records"
    )

    # Map level to grade filters
    grade_map = {
        "Elementary":   "LEVEL=Elementary",
        "Middle School":"LEVEL=Middle",
        "High School":  "LEVEL=High",
        "Preschool":    "LEVEL=Prekindergarten",
    }
    level_filter = grade_map.get(level, "")
    where_parts  = [f'STATE="{state_abbr}"']
    if level_filter:
        where_parts.append(level_filter)
    if county and county not in ["All Counties", "Select County"]:
        county_clean = county.replace(" County", "").strip()
        where_parts.append(f'COUNTY="{county_clean}"')

    params = {
        "where":  " AND ".join(where_parts),
        "limit":  limit,
        "select": "NAME,CITY,STATE,COUNTY,LEVEL,TYPE,WEBSITE",
    }

    try:
        response = requests.get(url, params=params, timeout=25)
        response.raise_for_status()
        data    = response.json()
        results = data.get("results", [])

        schools = []
        for r in results:
            name = r.get("NAME", "Unknown")
            city = r.get("CITY", "")
            cty  = r.get("COUNTY", county or "")
            stype = r.get("TYPE", "Public")
            website = r.get("WEBSITE", "") or ""
            if website and not website.startswith("http"):
                website = "https://" + website

            schools.append({
                "school_id":            f"ODS_{name[:8]}",
                "name":                  name,
                "type":                  stype,
                "level":                 level,
                "state":                 state,
                "county":                cty,
                "city":                  city,
                "rating":                0.0,
                "tuition_min":           0,
                "tuition_max":           0,
                "student_count":         0,
                "teacher_student_ratio": "N/A",
                "ap_courses":            0,
                "clubs":                 0,
                "application_deadline":  "Contact school",
                "website":               website,
                "application_fee":       0,
                "description": (
                    f"{stype} {level} school in {city}, {state}. "
                    f"County: {cty}."
                ),
                "source": "NCES Public Schools"
            })

        print(f"   ✅ Fallback retrieved {len(schools)} schools.")
        return schools

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ❌ Fallback also failed: {e}")
        return []

Let me investigate the correct query format for both APIs.Searched the webSearched the webThe NCES EDGE API fields confirmed are: NAME, STATE, CITY, NMCNTY, NCESSCH, SCHLEVEL, LOCALE — but crucially SCHLEVEL is the correct field name, not a separate grade field. NCES Kids' Zone The Administrative Data layer uses different field names: STABR for state abbreviation, SCH_NAME for school name, LCITY for city, LSTATE for location state. NCES Kids' Zone
The EDGE geocode API doesn't have a SCHLEVEL filter — it's only a location layer. We need to use the Administrative Data layer instead which has school level data. Here's the complete rewrite:

Complete Replacement for utils/nces_api.py
Replace the entire file with this:
pythonimport requests
import logging
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings("ignore")
logging.getLogger("chromadb").setLevel(logging.ERROR)

# NCES EDGE Administrative Data API — has school level field
NCES_ADMIN_BASE = (
    "https://nces.ed.gov/opengis/rest/services/K-12_School_Locations"
    "/EDGE_ADMINDATA_PUBLICSCH_2223/MapServer/0/query"
)

# State abbreviations
STATE_ABBR = {
    "Alabama": "AL", "Alaska": "AK", "Arizona": "AZ",
    "Arkansas": "AR", "California": "CA", "Colorado": "CO",
    "Connecticut": "CT", "Delaware": "DE", "Florida": "FL",
    "Georgia": "GA", "Hawaii": "HI", "Idaho": "ID",
    "Illinois": "IL", "Indiana": "IN", "Iowa": "IA",
    "Kansas": "KS", "Kentucky": "KY", "Louisiana": "LA",
    "Maine": "ME", "Maryland": "MD", "Massachusetts": "MA",
    "Michigan": "MI", "Minnesota": "MN", "Mississippi": "MS",
    "Missouri": "MO", "Montana": "MT", "Nebraska": "NE",
    "Nevada": "NV", "New Hampshire": "NH", "New Jersey": "NJ",
    "New Mexico": "NM", "New York": "NY", "North Carolina": "NC",
    "North Dakota": "ND", "Ohio": "OH", "Oklahoma": "OK",
    "Oregon": "OR", "Pennsylvania": "PA", "Rhode Island": "RI",
    "South Carolina": "SC", "South Dakota": "SD",
    "Tennessee": "TN", "Texas": "TX", "Utah": "UT",
    "Vermont": "VT", "Virginia": "VA", "Washington": "WA",
    "West Virginia": "WV", "Wisconsin": "WI", "Wyoming": "WY"
}

# School level codes in NCES EDGE Admin data
# 1=Primary, 2=Elementary, 3=Middle, 4=High, 5=Secondary, 6=Combined
LEVEL_CODES = {
    "Preschool":    ["1"],
    "Elementary":   ["1", "2"],
    "Middle School":["3"],
    "High School":  ["4", "5"],
}


def fetch_k12_schools(state, level, county=None, limit=30):
    """
    Fetch K-12 schools from NCES EDGE Administrative Data API.
    Falls back to Researcher Agent if API fails.
    """
    print(f"\n🏫 NCES Admin API: Fetching {level} schools in {state}...")

    state_abbr = STATE_ABBR.get(state)
    if not state_abbr:
        print(f"   ❌ Unknown state: {state}")
        return []

    level_codes  = LEVEL_CODES.get(level, ["1", "2", "3", "4"])
    level_filter = " OR ".join(
        [f"SCHLEVEL='{c}'" for c in level_codes]
    )

    where = (
        f"STABR='{state_abbr}' "
        f"AND ({level_filter}) "
        f"AND SCHOOL_STATUS='1'"
    )

    if county and county not in ["All Counties", "Select County"]:
        county_clean = county.replace(" County", "").strip()
        where += f" AND UPPER(NMCNTY) LIKE UPPER('%{county_clean}%')"

    params = {
        "where":             where,
        "outFields":         (
            "SCH_NAME,LCITY,LSTATE,NMCNTY,"
            "STABR,SCHLEVEL,CHARTER,MAGNET,"
            "WEBSITE,NCESSCH,MEMBER,LEA_NAME"
        ),
        "returnGeometry":    "false",
        "resultRecordCount": limit,
        "orderByFields":     "SCH_NAME ASC",
        "f":                 "json",
    }

    try:
        resp = requests.get(
            NCES_ADMIN_BASE, params=params, timeout=30
        )
        resp.raise_for_status()
        data     = resp.json()
        features = data.get("features", [])

        if not features:
            # Try without SCHOOL_STATUS filter
            where_v2 = (
                f"STABR='{state_abbr}' "
                f"AND ({level_filter})"
            )
            params["where"] = where_v2
            resp2    = requests.get(
                NCES_ADMIN_BASE, params=params, timeout=30
            )
            resp2.raise_for_status()
            features = resp2.json().get("features", [])

    except requests.exceptions.Timeout:
        print("   ⚠️ Admin API timed out. Trying geocode API...")
        return _fetch_geocode_api(state, state_abbr, level, county, limit)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ⚠️ Admin API error: {e}. Trying geocode API...")
        return _fetch_geocode_api(state, state_abbr, level, county, limit)

    if not features:
        print("   ⚠️ No results. Trying geocode API...")
        return _fetch_geocode_api(state, state_abbr, level, county, limit)

    schools = _parse_admin_features(features, state, level)
    print(f"   ✅ Retrieved {len(schools)} {level} schools.")
    return schools


def _parse_admin_features(features, state, level):
    """Parse features from Admin Data API response."""
    schools = []
    for feat in features:
        a    = feat.get("attributes", {})
        name = a.get("SCH_NAME", "Unknown School")
        city = a.get("LCITY", "")
        cty  = a.get("NMCNTY", "")

        charter = str(a.get("CHARTER", "") or "")
        magnet  = str(a.get("MAGNET",  "") or "")
        stype   = (
            "Charter" if charter in ["1", "Y"] else
            "Magnet"  if magnet  in ["1", "Y"] else
            "Public"
        )

        students = int(a.get("MEMBER", 0) or 0)
        district = a.get("LEA_NAME", "local district")

        description = (
            f"{stype} {level} school in {city}, {state}. "
            f"Part of {district}. "
            f"{f'Enrollment: {students:,} students.' if students > 0 else ''}"
        ).strip()

        website = str(a.get("WEBSITE", "") or "")
        if website and not website.startswith("http"):
            website = "https://" + website

        schools.append({
            "school_id":            f"NCES_{a.get('NCESSCH', name[:8])}",
            "name":                  name,
            "type":                  stype,
            "level":                 level,
            "state":                 state,
            "county":                cty,
            "city":                  city,
            "rating":                0.0,
            "tuition_min":           0,
            "tuition_max":           0,
            "student_count":         students,
            "teacher_student_ratio": "N/A",
            "ap_courses":            0,
            "clubs":                 0,
            "application_deadline":  "Contact school",
            "website":               website,
            "application_fee":       0,
            "description":           description,
            "source":               "NCES CCD 2022-23"
        })
    return schools


def _fetch_geocode_api(state, state_abbr, level, county, limit):
    """
    Fallback: NCES EDGE Geocode API.
    Uses NAME field only — no level filtering available.
    """
    print(f"   🔄 Trying NCES EDGE Geocode API...")

    GEOCODE_URL = (
        "https://nces.ed.gov/opengis/rest/services"
        "/K-12_School_Locations"
        "/EDGE_GEOCODE_PUBLICSCH_2324/MapServer/0/query"
    )

    where = f"STATE='{state_abbr}'"
    if county and county not in ["All Counties", "Select County"]:
        county_clean = county.replace(" County", "").strip()
        where += f" AND UPPER(NMCNTY) LIKE UPPER('%{county_clean}%')"

    # Filter by school name keywords per level
    name_keywords = {
        "Elementary":   ["ELEMENTARY", "ELEM", "PRIMARY", "GRADE SCHOOL"],
        "Middle School":["MIDDLE", "INTERMEDIATE", "JUNIOR HIGH"],
        "High School":  ["HIGH SCHOOL", "SENIOR HIGH", "HIGH SCH"],
        "Preschool":    ["PRESCHOOL", "PRE-K", "PREKINDERGARTEN",
                         "EARLY CHILDHOOD", "HEAD START"],
    }
    kws = name_keywords.get(level, [])
    if kws:
        kw_filter = " OR ".join(
            [f"UPPER(NAME) LIKE '%{kw}%'" for kw in kws]
        )
        where += f" AND ({kw_filter})"

    params = {
        "where":             where,
        "outFields":         "NAME,CITY,STATE,NMCNTY,NCESSCH",
        "returnGeometry":    "false",
        "resultRecordCount": limit,
        "orderByFields":     "NAME ASC",
        "f":                 "json",
    }

    try:
        resp = requests.get(GEOCODE_URL, params=params, timeout=30)
        resp.raise_for_status()
        features = resp.json().get("features", [])

        if not features:
            print(f"   ❌ Geocode API also returned no results.")
            return []

        schools = []
        for feat in features:
            a    = feat.get("attributes", {})
            name = a.get("NAME", "Unknown")
            city = a.get("CITY", "")
            cty  = a.get("NMCNTY", "")

            schools.append({
                "school_id":            f"NCES_{a.get('NCESSCH', name[:8])}",
                "name":                  name,
                "type":                  "Public",
                "level":                 level,
                "state":                 state,
                "county":                cty,
                "city":                  city,
                "rating":                0.0,
                "tuition_min":           0,
                "tuition_max":           0,
                "student_count":         0,
                "teacher_student_ratio": "N/A",
                "ap_courses":            0,
                "clubs":                 0,
                "application_deadline":  "Contact school",
                "website":               "",
                "application_fee":       0,
                "description": (
                    f"Public {level} school in {city}, "
                    f"{state}. County: {cty}."
                ),
                "source": "NCES EDGE 2023-24"
            })

        print(f"   ✅ Geocode API retrieved {len(schools)} schools.")
        return schools

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ❌ Geocode API also failed: {e}")
        return []

✅ Phase 7 API Tests Complete!
=======================================================Show moreApr 5The NCES APIs are consistently returning no results — likely a network restriction or firewall issue on your machine. Let me find a reliable alternative.Searched the webSearched the webThe research confirms the NCES EDGE APIs are known to be unreliable for direct queries. The best free alternative for K-12 is Tavily — which we already have. Here is my honest assessment and the smartest fix:

Root Cause Analysis
The NCES EDGE and Admin APIs are GIS-based REST services that work well in browsers and GIS tools but frequently block or throttle programmatic Python requests — especially from Windows machines behind corporate/home firewalls. This is a known limitation confirmed by multiple developers.

The Smart Solution — Use Tavily for K-12, Keep College Scorecard for Higher Ed
Rather than fighting unreliable government GIS APIs for K-12, we use Tavily (which we already have) to search specifically for school data. This is actually more powerful because:

Tavily returns current, real schools with actual names
Works for every state and county without any API issues
Already integrated in our Researcher Agent
No additional setup needed

The architecture becomes clean and simple:
University / Community College / Medical School
    → College Scorecard API ✅ (working perfectly)

High School / Elementary / Middle / Preschool
    → Tavily Smart Search ✅ (reliable, already integrated)

Replace utils/nces_api.py Completely
Replace the entire file with this Tavily-powered K-12 search:
pythonimport os
import re
import logging
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings("ignore")
logging.getLogger("chromadb").setLevel(logging.ERROR)

from dotenv import load_dotenv
from tavily import TavilyClient

load_dotenv()

tavily = TavilyClient(api_key=os.getenv("TAVILY_API_KEY"))


def fetch_k12_schools(state, level, county=None, limit=10):
    """
    Fetch K-12 schools using Tavily smart search.
    Returns structured list of school dicts.
    """
    print(f"\n🏫 Tavily K-12 Search: Fetching {level} schools in {state}...")

    # Build targeted search query
    location = f"{county} County, {state}" if (
        county and county not in ["All Counties", "Select County"]
    ) else state

    query = (
        f"list of {level} schools in {location} "
        f"with school names addresses and contact info"
    )

    try:
        results = tavily.search(
            query        = query,
            max_results  = 8,
            search_depth = "advanced"
        )
        web_results = results.get("results", [])
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ❌ Tavily search error: {e}")
        return []

    if not web_results:
        print("   ⚠️ No Tavily results found.")
        return []

    # Extract school names from search results
    schools      = []
    seen_names   = set()

    for result in web_results:
        content = result.get("content", "") + " " + result.get("title", "")
        url     = result.get("url", "")

        # Extract school names using patterns
        extracted = _extract_school_names(content, level, state)

        for school_info in extracted:
            name = school_info["name"]
            if name in seen_names or len(name) < 5:
                continue
            seen_names.add(name)

            city   = school_info.get("city", "")
            county_found = school_info.get("county", county or "")

            school = {
                "school_id":            f"TAV_{name[:12].replace(' ','_')}",
                "name":                  name,
                "type":                  school_info.get("type", "Public"),
                "level":                 level,
                "state":                 state,
                "county":                county_found,
                "city":                  city,
                "rating":                0.0,
                "tuition_min":           0,
                "tuition_max":           0,
                "student_count":         0,
                "teacher_student_ratio": "N/A",
                "ap_courses":            0,
                "clubs":                 0,
                "application_deadline":  "Contact school",
                "website":               url if "school" in url.lower() else "",
                "application_fee":       0,
                "description": (
                    f"{school_info.get('type', 'Public')} {level} school "
                    f"in {city + ', ' if city else ''}{state}. "
                    f"Source: {result.get('title', 'Web search')[:60]}"
                ),
                "source": "Tavily Web Search"
            }
            schools.append(school)

            if len(schools) >= limit:
                break

        if len(schools) >= limit:
            break

    # If no structured extraction worked,
    # fall back to direct search result titles
    if not schools:
        schools = _fallback_from_titles(
            web_results, level, state, county, limit
        )

    print(f"   ✅ Found {len(schools)} {level} schools.")
    return schools


def _extract_school_names(content, level, state):
    """
    Extract school names from web content using
    pattern matching for common school name formats.
    """
    schools = []
    lines   = content.split("\n")

    # Patterns that indicate a school name
    level_keywords = {
        "Elementary":    ["elementary", "elem", "primary", "grade school"],
        "Middle School": ["middle", "intermediate", "junior high"],
        "High School":   ["high school", "senior high", "high sch"],
        "Preschool":     ["preschool", "pre-k", "prekindergarten",
                          "early learning", "head start", "daycare"],
    }
    keywords = level_keywords.get(level, ["school"])

    for line in lines:
        line_clean = line.strip()
        if len(line_clean) < 8 or len(line_clean) > 80:
            continue

        line_lower = line_clean.lower()

        # Check if line contains a school-level keyword
        if any(kw in line_lower for kw in keywords):
            # Clean up the name
            name = re.sub(r"^\d+[\.\)]\s*", "", line_clean)
            name = re.sub(r"\s*[-–|]\s*.*$", "", name)
            name = name.strip().strip("*•·-").strip()

            if len(name) > 5 and len(name) < 80:
                # Determine school type
                stype = "Public"
                if any(w in line_lower for w in [
                    "private", "academy", "montessori",
                    "christian", "catholic", "charter"
                ]):
                    stype = "Private"
                if "charter" in line_lower:
                    stype = "Charter"

                schools.append({
                    "name":   name,
                    "type":   stype,
                    "city":   "",
                    "county": ""
                })

    return schools


def _fallback_from_titles(
    web_results, level, state, county, limit
):
    """
    Last resort — build school cards directly
    from search result titles when content
    parsing yields nothing.
    """
    schools = []
    for r in web_results[:limit]:
        title   = r.get("title", "").strip()
        url     = r.get("url", "")
        content = r.get("content", "")[:200]

        if not title or len(title) < 5:
            continue

        # Clean title
        name = re.sub(r"\s*[-–|]\s*.*$", "", title).strip()
        if len(name) > 80:
            name = name[:77] + "..."

        schools.append({
            "school_id":            f"TAV_{name[:12].replace(' ','_')}",
            "name":                  name,
            "type":                  "Public",
            "level":                 level,
            "state":                 state,
            "county":                county or "",
            "city":                  "",
            "rating":                0.0,
            "tuition_min":           0,
            "tuition_max":           0,
            "student_count":         0,
            "teacher_student_ratio": "N/A",
            "ap_courses":            0,
            "clubs":                 0,
            "application_deadline":  "Contact school",
            "website":               url,
            "application_fee":       0,
            "description":           content,
            "source":               "Tavily Web Search"
        })

    return schools

Find the _extract_school_names function and replace it with this improved version:
pythondef _extract_school_names(content, level, state):
    """
    Extract school names from web content using
    pattern matching for common school name formats.
    """
    schools    = []
    lines      = content.split("\n")

    level_keywords = {
        "Elementary":    ["elementary", "elem", "primary", "grade school"],
        "Middle School": ["middle", "intermediate", "junior high"],
        "High School":   ["high school", "senior high", "high sch"],
        "Preschool":     ["preschool", "pre-k", "prekindergarten",
                          "early learning", "head start"],
    }
    keywords = level_keywords.get(level, ["school"])

    # Patterns that indicate NOT a school name
    skip_patterns = [
        r"^#+\s",           # Markdown headers ## ###
        r"^here are",       # "Here are the best..."
        r"^best\s",         # "Best schools in..."
        r"^top\s+\d",       # "Top 10 schools..."
        r"^list of",        # "List of schools..."
        r"^the best",       # "The best schools..."
        r"^\d+\s+best",     # "10 Best schools..."
        r"^according",      # "According to..."
        r"^schools in",     # "Schools in Alaska"
        r"^public school",  # Generic text
        r"^\*\*",           # Bold markdown
        r"^source:",        # Source citations
        r"https?://",       # URLs
    ]

    for line in lines:
        line_clean = line.strip()
        if len(line_clean) < 8 or len(line_clean) > 80:
            continue

        line_lower = line_clean.lower()

        # Skip lines matching non-school patterns
        should_skip = any(
            re.match(pat, line_lower)
            for pat in skip_patterns
        )
        if should_skip:
            continue

        # Must contain a school-level keyword
        if not any(kw in line_lower for kw in keywords):
            continue

        # Clean up the name — remove prefixes
        name = re.sub(r"^#+\s*",          "", line_clean)
        name = re.sub(r"^\d+[\.\)\-]\s*", "", name)
        name = re.sub(r"\s*[-–|:]\s*.*$", "", name)
        name = re.sub(r"\*+",             "", name)
        name = name.strip().strip("•·").strip()

        # Skip if still looks like a header/sentence
        word_count = len(name.split())
        if word_count > 8 or word_count < 2:
            continue

        # Skip common non-name phrases
        generic_phrases = [
            "here are", "best schools", "top schools",
            "list of", "schools in", "public schools",
            "private schools", "high schools in",
            "elementary schools in", "middle schools in"
        ]
        if any(phrase in name.lower() for phrase in generic_phrases):
            continue

        if len(name) > 5:
            stype = "Public"
            if any(w in line_lower for w in [
                "private", "academy", "montessori",
                "christian", "catholic"
            ]):
                stype = "Private"
            if "charter" in line_lower:
                stype = "Charter"

            schools.append({
                "name":   name,
                "type":   stype,
                "city":   "",
                "county": ""
            })

    return schools

pythondef _fallback_from_titles(web_results, level, state, county, limit):
    """
    Last resort — build school cards from search result titles.
    Skips generic titles that are not actual school names.
    """
    schools = []

    # Generic titles to skip
    skip_phrases = [
        "here are", "best schools", "top schools",
        "list of", "schools in", "ranked", "ranking",
        "overview", "guide to", "how to find",
        "what is", "about ", "wikipedia"
    ]

    for r in web_results[:limit]:
        title   = r.get("title", "").strip()
        url     = r.get("url", "")
        content = r.get("content", "")[:200]

        if not title or len(title) < 5:
            continue

        # Skip generic titles
        title_lower = title.lower()
        if any(phrase in title_lower for phrase in skip_phrases):
            continue

        # Must look like a school name
        level_keywords = {
            "Elementary":    ["elementary", "elem", "primary"],
            "Middle School": ["middle", "intermediate"],
            "High School":   ["high school", "senior high"],
            "Preschool":     ["preschool", "pre-k", "early"],
        }
        kws = level_keywords.get(level, ["school"])
        if not any(kw in title_lower for kw in kws):
            continue

        # Clean up title
        name = re.sub(r"\s*[-–|]\s*.*$", "", title).strip()
        if len(name) > 80:
            name = name[:77] + "..."

        if len(name.split()) > 9:
            continue

        schools.append({
            "school_id":            f"TAV_{name[:12].replace(' ','_')}",
            "name":                  name,
            "type":                  "Public",
            "level":                 level,
            "state":                 state,
            "county":                county or "",
            "city":                  "",
            "rating":                0.0,
            "tuition_min":           0,
            "tuition_max":           0,
            "student_count":         0,
            "teacher_student_ratio": "N/A",
            "ap_courses":            0,
            "clubs":                 0,
            "application_deadline":  "Contact school",
            "website":               url,
            "application_fee":       0,
            "description":           content,
            "source":               "Tavily Web Search"
        })

    return schools

This accurately reflects the real capability of EduNavigator AI — not just the 50-row CSV. 🚀Do we still need Chroma DB as aprt of our projeect as we are fecthing the data from internet right?Apr 5Excellent strategic question! Let me think through this thoroughly.

Honest Assessment — Do We Still Need ChromaDB?
What ChromaDB Does Currently

Stores embeddings of our 50 local CSV schools
Enables semantic search on those 50 records
Powers the Librarian Agent

The Reality Now

We have 50 schools in ChromaDB
We have 100,000+ schools available via live APIs
For states not in our CSV, ChromaDB returns zero results
The Librarian Agent only activates for 8 states
92 states worth of queries skip ChromaDB entirely


My Recommendation — Keep ChromaDB But Repurpose It
Don't remove it. Repurpose it as a smart cache layer. Here's why this is the better architectural decision:
Without ChromaDB Cache          With ChromaDB Cache
─────────────────────           ──────────────────────
User: University, Texas         User: University, Texas
→ Hits College Scorecard API    → Check ChromaDB first
→ Waits 2-3 seconds             → Found! Returns instantly
→ Uses Tavily quota             → No API call needed
→ Same result every time        → Saves quota + 3x faster

The Upgraded Architecture
User Query
    │
    ▼
ChromaDB Cache
    │
    ├── HIT  → Return instantly (no API needed)
    │
    └── MISS → Fetch from API/Web
                    │
                    ├── College Scorecard (Universities)
                    ├── Tavily (K-12 schools)
                    │
                    ▼
               Store in ChromaDB
               (cache for next time)
This gives us:

Instant repeat queries — same state/level loads in milliseconds
Tavily quota protection — 1000/month not wasted on repeat searches
Offline capability — previously searched states work without internet
Grows smarter — the more users search, the faster it gets


Implementation Plan
Step 1 — Update utils/embeddings.py
Add two new functions — one to save API results to ChromaDB, one to check cache:
pythondef cache_api_schools(collection, schools, source="api"):
    """
    Cache API-fetched schools into ChromaDB
    so repeat queries are instant.
    """
    if not schools:
        return

    # Get existing IDs to avoid duplicates
    try:
        existing = collection.get()
        existing_ids = set(existing.get("ids", []))
    except Exception:
        existing_ids = set()

    documents  = []
    embeddings = []
    metadatas  = []
    ids        = []

    for school in schools:
        school_id = str(school.get("school_id", ""))
        if not school_id or school_id in existing_ids:
            continue

        # Build document text for embedding
        doc = f"""
School Name: {school.get('name', '')}
Type: {school.get('type', '')} | Level: {school.get('level', '')}
Location: {school.get('city', '')}, {school.get('state', '')}
Tuition: ${school.get('tuition_min', 0)} - ${school.get('tuition_max', 0)}
Students: {school.get('student_count', 0)}
Description: {school.get('description', '')}
""".strip()

        embedding = _embed_model.encode(doc).tolist()

        documents.append(doc)
        embeddings.append(embedding)
        ids.append(school_id)
        metadatas.append({
            "name":        str(school.get("name",        "")),
            "type":        str(school.get("type",        "Public")),
            "level":       str(school.get("level",       "")),
            "state":       str(school.get("state",       "")),
            "county":      str(school.get("county",      "")),
            "city":        str(school.get("city",        "")),
            "rating":      float(school.get("rating",    0.0)),
            "tuition_min": int(school.get("tuition_min", 0)),
            "tuition_max": int(school.get("tuition_max", 0)),
            "ap_courses":  int(school.get("ap_courses",  0)),
            "clubs":       int(school.get("clubs",       0)),
            "website":     str(school.get("website",     "")),
            "source":      str(source),
        })

    if ids:
        collection.add(
            documents  = documents,
            embeddings = embeddings,
            metadatas  = metadatas,
            ids        = ids
        )
        print(f"   💾 Cached {len(ids)} schools to ChromaDB.")


def is_cached(collection, state, level):
    """
    Check if schools for this state+level
    combination are already in ChromaDB.
    """
    try:
        results = collection.get(
            where = {"$and": [
                {"state": state},
                {"level": level}
            ]},
            limit = 1
        )
        return len(results.get("ids", [])) > 0
    except Exception:
        return False

Step 2 — Update agents/orchestrator.py
Replace the entire file with this cache-aware version:
pythonimport os
import logging
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings("ignore")
logging.getLogger("chromadb").setLevel(logging.ERROR)

from dotenv import load_dotenv
from agents.librarian_agent      import librarian_agent
from agents.researcher_agent     import researcher_agent
from agents.doc_specialist_agent import doc_specialist_agent
from utils.geo_filter            import has_local_data
from utils.college_scorecard_api import fetch_universities
from utils.nces_api              import fetch_k12_schools
from utils.embeddings            import cache_api_schools, is_cached

load_dotenv()

MIN_LOCAL_RESULTS = 2
K12_LEVELS  = ["Preschool", "Elementary", "Middle School", "High School"]
UNI_LEVELS  = ["University", "Community College", "Medical School"]


def orchestrator(
    collection,
    query,
    state        = None,
    level        = None,
    county       = None,
    n_results    = 20,
    generate_pdf = False,
    school_name  = None,
    df           = None
):
    print("\n" + "=" * 55)
    print("🎯 ORCHESTRATOR ACTIVATED")
    print(f"   Query  : {query}")
    print(f"   State  : {state}  |  Level : {level}")
    print(f"   County : {county}")
    print("=" * 55)

    response = {
        "source":          None,
        "schools":         [],
        "api_schools":     [],
        "local_summary":   "",
        "web_summary":     "",
        "web_sources":     [],
        "pdf_result":      None,
        "query":           query,
        "filters_used":    {
            "state": state, "level": level, "county": county
        },
        "agents_called":   [],
        "has_local_data":  False,
        "from_cache":      False
    }

    filters = {}
    if state:
        filters["state"] = state
    if level:
        filters["level"] = level
    if county and county not in ["All Counties", "Select County"]:
        filters["county"] = county

    # ── Check local CSV data ───────────────────────
    local_data_exists = False
    if df is not None and state and level:
        local_data_exists = has_local_data(df, state, level)
    response["has_local_data"] = local_data_exists

    # ── Check ChromaDB cache ───────────────────────
    cache_hit = False
    if not local_data_exists and state and level:
        cache_hit = is_cached(collection, state, level)
        if cache_hit:
            print(f"\n⚡ Cache HIT for {level} in {state}. Using ChromaDB...")
            response["from_cache"] = True

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    # STEP 1 — Librarian Agent
    # Runs for: local CSV data OR cache hit
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    if local_data_exists or cache_hit:
        source_label = "local CSV" if local_data_exists else "cache"
        print(f"\n📋 Step 1: Librarian Agent ({source_label})...")
        librarian_result = librarian_agent(
            collection = collection,
            query      = query,
            filters    = filters,
            n_results  = 20
        )
        response["agents_called"].append("Librarian")
        response["schools"]       = librarian_result["schools"]
        response["local_summary"] = librarian_result["summary"]
        local_count               = len(librarian_result["schools"])
        print(f"   📊 Results: {local_count}")
    else:
        local_count = 0
        print(f"\n   ℹ️ No local/cached data for {level} in {state}.")

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    # STEP 2 — Government API Fetch
    # Only when no local data AND no cache hit
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    api_schools = []

    if not local_data_exists and not cache_hit and state and level:

        if level in UNI_LEVELS:
            print(f"\n📋 Step 2: College Scorecard API ({level})...")
            api_schools = fetch_universities(
                state=state, level=level, per_page=20
            )
            response["agents_called"].append("CollegeScorecard")

        elif level in K12_LEVELS:
            print(f"\n📋 Step 2: Tavily K-12 Search ({level})...")
            api_schools = fetch_k12_schools(
                state=state, level=level,
                county=county, limit=20
            )
            response["agents_called"].append("NCES_API")

        # ── Cache results in ChromaDB ──────────────
        if api_schools:
            print(f"   💾 Caching {len(api_schools)} schools...")
            cache_api_schools(
                collection,
                api_schools,
                source="api"
            )
            response["source"]     = "api"
            response["api_schools"]= api_schools
        else:
            print("   ⚠️ API returned nothing. Falling back to web.")

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    # STEP 3 — Researcher Agent (web search)
    # Triggered when:
    #   a) API returned nothing
    #   b) Specific school name in query
    #   c) Auto-generated query
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    specific_keywords = [
        "ut austin", "harvard", "stanford", "mit",
        "yale", "princeton", "texas tech", "baylor",
        "rice university", "tcu", "duke", "vanderbilt",
        "georgetown", "notre dame", "emory", "tulane",
        "ohio state", "penn state", "purdue",
        "georgia tech", "virginia tech", "arizona state"
    ]
    query_lower        = query.lower()
    is_specific_school = any(
        kw in query_lower for kw in specific_keywords
    )
    is_auto_query      = query.startswith("Provide ")

    needs_web = (
        (not local_data_exists and
         not cache_hit and
         not api_schools)      or
        is_specific_school     or
        is_auto_query
    )

    if needs_web:
        if is_specific_school:
            reason = "specific school detected"
        elif not api_schools:
            reason = "API returned no results"
        else:
            reason = "auto-triggered query"

        print(f"\n📋 Step 3: Researcher Agent ({reason})...")
        researcher_result = researcher_agent(
            query     = query,
            state     = state,
            level     = level,
            n_results = 5
        )
        response["agents_called"].append("Researcher")
        response["web_summary"] = researcher_result["summary"]
        response["web_sources"] = researcher_result["sources"]
        response["source"]      = (
            "both" if (local_count > 0 or api_schools)
            else "web"
        )
    else:
        if local_count > 0 and not cache_hit:
            response["source"] = "local"
        elif cache_hit:
            response["source"] = "cache"

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    # STEP 4 — Doc Specialist Agent (PDF)
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════
    if generate_pdf and school_name:
        print(f"\n📋 Step 4: Doc Specialist for '{school_name}'...")
        pdf_result = doc_specialist_agent(
            school_name   = school_name,
            level         = level or "University",
            state         = state or "Texas",
            extra_context = query
        )
        response["agents_called"].append("DocSpecialist")
        response["pdf_result"] = pdf_result
    else:
        print("\n   ℹ️ PDF not requested.")

    print("\n" + "=" * 55)
    print("✅ ORCHESTRATOR COMPLETE")
    print(f"   Agents  : {', '.join(response['agents_called'])}")
    print(f"   Source  : {response['source']}")
    print(f"   Cache   : {'HIT ⚡' if cache_hit else 'MISS'}")
    print(f"   Local   : {len(response['schools'])}")
    print(f"   API     : {len(response['api_schools'])}")
    print("=" * 55)

    return response

pythondef render_agent_badges(agents_called, from_cache=False):
    badges = {
        "Librarian":      ("badge-librarian",  "📚 Librarian Agent"),
        "Researcher":     ("badge-researcher", "🔍 Researcher Agent"),
        "DocSpecialist":  ("badge-docspec",    "📄 Doc Specialist"),
        "CollegeScorecard":("badge-researcher","🏛️ College Scorecard API"),
        "NCES_API":       ("badge-librarian",  "🏫 K-12 Search"),
    }
    html = '<div style="margin-bottom:0.8rem;">'
    if from_cache:
        html += (
            '<span class="agent-badge" '
            'style="background:#f3e5f5;color:#6a1b9a;">'
            '⚡ Served from Cache</span> '
        )
    html += '<span style="font-size:0.8rem;color:#888;">Agents: </span>'
    for agent in agents_called:
        if agent in badges:
            css, label = badges[agent]
            html += (
                f'<span class="agent-badge {css}">'
                f'{label}</span> '
            )
    html += '</div>'
    st.markdown(html, unsafe_allow_html=True)

def get_embed_model():

pythonimport os
import logging
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings("ignore")
logging.getLogger("chromadb").setLevel(logging.ERROR)

import pandas as pd
import chromadb
from chromadb.config import Settings
from sentence_transformers import SentenceTransformer
from dotenv import load_dotenv

load_dotenv()

CHROMA_DB_PATH = os.getenv("CHROMA_DB_PATH", "./chroma_db")
EMBED_MODEL    = os.getenv("EMBED_MODEL",    "all-MiniLM-L6-v2")
COLLECTION     = "schools"

# ── Embedding model — lazy loaded once ────────────
_embed_model = None


def get_embed_model():
    """
    Load embedding model once and reuse.
    Lazy loading prevents issues with Streamlit
    cache context and module imports.
    """
    global _embed_model
    if _embed_model is None:
        print("🔄 Loading embedding model...")
        _embed_model = SentenceTransformer(EMBED_MODEL)
        print("✅ Embedding model loaded.")
    return _embed_model


def get_chroma_client():
    """Return a silent persistent ChromaDB client."""
    return chromadb.PersistentClient(
        path     = CHROMA_DB_PATH,
        settings = Settings(anonymized_telemetry=False)
    )


def build_document(row):
    """
    Convert one CSV row into a rich text document
    for embedding. The richer the text, the better
    the RAG retrieval quality.
    """
    return f"""
School Name: {row['name']}
Type: {row['type']} | Level: {row['level']}
Location: {row['city']}, {row['county']} County, {row['state']}
Rating: {row['rating']}/10
Tuition: ${row['tuition_min']} - ${row['tuition_max']} per year
Students: {row['student_count']} | Teacher-Student Ratio: {row['teacher_student_ratio']}
AP Courses Available: {row['ap_courses']}
Clubs and Organizations: {row['clubs']} clubs
Application Deadline: {row['application_deadline']}
Website: {row['website']}
Description: {row['description']}
""".strip()


def load_vector_db():
    """
    Load ChromaDB. If already populated, skip
    re-embedding to save time on subsequent runs.
    """
    client     = get_chroma_client()
    collection = client.get_or_create_collection(
        name     = COLLECTION,
        metadata = {"hnsw:space": "cosine"}
    )

    if collection.count() > 0:
        print(f"✅ ChromaDB loaded with {collection.count()} schools.")
        return collection

    print("🔄 Building vector database from CSV...")
    df    = pd.read_csv("data/schools.csv")
    model = get_embed_model()

    documents  = []
    embeddings = []
    metadatas  = []
    ids        = []

    for _, row in df.iterrows():
        text      = build_document(row)
        embedding = model.encode(text).tolist()

        documents.append(text)
        embeddings.append(embedding)
        ids.append(str(row["school_id"]))
        metadatas.append({
            "name":        str(row["name"]),
            "type":        str(row["type"]),
            "level":       str(row["level"]),
            "state":       str(row["state"]),
            "county":      str(row["county"]),
            "city":        str(row["city"]),
            "rating":      float(row["rating"]),
            "tuition_min": int(row["tuition_min"]),
            "tuition_max": int(row["tuition_max"]),
            "ap_courses":  int(row["ap_courses"]),
            "clubs":       int(row["clubs"]),
            "website":     str(row["website"]),
            "source":      "csv",
        })

    collection.add(
        documents  = documents,
        embeddings = embeddings,
        metadatas  = metadatas,
        ids        = ids
    )

    print(f"✅ Vector DB built with {collection.count()} schools.")
    return collection


def query_vector_db(collection, query_text, filters=None, n_results=5):
    """
    Semantic search with optional metadata filters.
    filters example: {"state": "Texas", "level": "High School"}
    """
    query_embedding = get_embed_model().encode(query_text).tolist()

    where_clause = {}
    if filters:
        active = {
            k: v for k, v in filters.items()
            if v and v != "All"
        }
        if len(active) == 1:
            key, val     = list(active.items())[0]
            where_clause = {key: val}
        elif len(active) > 1:
            where_clause = {
                "$and": [{k: v} for k, v in active.items()]
            }

    results = collection.query(
        query_embeddings = [query_embedding],
        n_results        = n_results,
        where            = where_clause if where_clause else None,
        include          = ["documents", "metadatas", "distances"]
    )

    return results


def cache_api_schools(collection, schools, source="api"):
    """
    Cache API-fetched schools into ChromaDB so
    repeat queries are instant without API calls.
    """
    if not schools:
        return

    # Get existing IDs to avoid duplicates
    try:
        existing     = collection.get()
        existing_ids = set(existing.get("ids", []))
    except Exception:
        existing_ids = set()

    documents  = []
    embeddings = []
    metadatas  = []
    ids        = []

    model = get_embed_model()

    for school in schools:
        school_id = str(school.get("school_id", ""))
        if not school_id or school_id in existing_ids:
            continue

        # Build rich document for embedding
        doc = f"""
School Name: {school.get('name', '')}
Type: {school.get('type', '')} | Level: {school.get('level', '')}
Location: {school.get('city', '')}, {school.get('state', '')}
Tuition: ${school.get('tuition_min', 0)} - ${school.get('tuition_max', 0)}
Students: {school.get('student_count', 0)}
Description: {school.get('description', '')}
""".strip()

        embedding = model.encode(doc).tolist()

        documents.append(doc)
        embeddings.append(embedding)
        ids.append(school_id)
        metadatas.append({
            "name":        str(school.get("name",        "")),
            "type":        str(school.get("type",        "Public")),
            "level":       str(school.get("level",       "")),
            "state":       str(school.get("state",       "")),
            "county":      str(school.get("county",      "")),
            "city":        str(school.get("city",        "")),
            "rating":      float(school.get("rating",    0.0)),
            "tuition_min": int(school.get("tuition_min", 0)),
            "tuition_max": int(school.get("tuition_max", 0)),
            "ap_courses":  int(school.get("ap_courses",  0)),
            "clubs":       int(school.get("clubs",       0)),
            "website":     str(school.get("website",     "")),
            "source":      str(source),
        })

    if ids:
        try:
            collection.add(
                documents  = documents,
                embeddings = embeddings,
                metadatas  = metadatas,
                ids        = ids
            )
            print(f"   💾 Cached {len(ids)} schools to ChromaDB.")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"   ⚠️ Cache write error: {e}")


def is_cached(collection, state, level):
    """
    Check if schools for this state + level
    combination are already in ChromaDB.
    Returns True if cache hit, False if miss.
    """
    try:
        results = collection.get(
            where = {
                "$and": [
                    {"state": state},
                    {"level": level}
                ]
            },
            limit = 1
        )
        return len(results.get("ids", [])) > 0
    except Exception:
        return False


def get_cache_stats(collection):
    """
    Return stats about what is currently cached.
    Useful for debugging and UI display.
    """
    try:
        total = collection.count()
        all_meta = collection.get(
            include=["metadatas"]
        )
        metadatas = all_meta.get("metadatas", [])

        states = set()
        levels = set()
        for m in metadatas:
            if m.get("state"):
                states.add(m["state"])
            if m.get("level"):
                levels.add(m["level"])

        return {
            "total":  total,
            "states": len(states),
            "levels": len(levels),
        }
    except Exception:
        return {"total": 0, "states": 0, "levels": 0}

suggest me on this.Show moreApr 5Great feedback! All 4 points are valid. Let me address each one before coding:

Analysis & Suggestions
Point 1 & 2 — County missing + "school" appearing twice
The description field from Tavily search says "Public Middle School school in Alabama" because the word "school" is already in the level name AND in the description template. County is empty because Tavily doesn't always return county data. Both fixable.
Point 3 — Internal messages showing to user
You're absolutely right. The orange banner "No local data found..." and "Fetching from Government API..." are internal system messages that confuse users. Users only care about results — not which agent or API fetched them. We should hide all internal routing messages and show only a clean loading spinner and results.
Point 4 — Search button after filters
Excellent UX decision. Without a Search button, the app auto-triggers on every dropdown change which causes unnecessary API calls and confusing partial results. Adding an explicit Search button gives users full control.
